As for the negotiations with the South Manchuria Railway regarding the repair of vehicles and the purchase of locomotives, there were no significant results. The Jiaoji (Jiaozhou-Jinan) Railway had previously had the South Manchuria Railway manufacture four locomotives, each costing 30,000 Japanese yen, which was cheaper than Western products. Therefore, the Tianjin-Pukou Railway intended to continue the Jiaoji Railway's contract and have the South Manchuria Railway manufacture several locomotives. However, the South Manchuria Railway claimed that the locomotives manufactured for the Jiaoji Railway had already resulted in losses and they could no longer manufacture them at that price. If they were to manufacture them, the price per locomotive would have to be increased to 35,000 yen, which was too high, so no agreement was reached. In addition, they requested the South Manchuria Railway to repair vehicles, but the price set by the South Manchuria Railway was also very expensive. Even the Japanese said it was not cost-effective and advised against repairing them, so that was also abandoned. There are plans to have the South Manchuria Railway send people to the Tianjin-Pukou Railway to inspect the vehicles that need to be repaired so that a long-term plan can be made. (March 10)

Harbin Merchants Request Reduction of Freight Rates on the East Manchuria and South Manchuria Railways 57

While also requesting the speedy construction of the Harbin-Taonan Railway. A dispatch from Harbin reports that today, eight organizations, including the Harbin Municipal Chamber of Commerce, submitted a joint petition to the Special Region Administrative Chief's Office requesting a letter be forwarded to the Chinese Eastern Railway Bureau and the Manchuria Railway Office to reduce freight rates. They also scheduled a meeting for representatives from various organizations to submit a petition to the Eastern Railway Bureau and the Manchuria Railway Office on the 9th of this month. If no results are achieved, they will proceed with issuing 10 million in public bonds to build a section of the railway between Harbin and Taonan in order to bypass the East Manchuria and South Manchuria Railways. The text of their petition to the Administrative Chief's Office is as follows:

"The Chinese Eastern and South Manchuria Railways are connected and run through the north and south of the three provinces. They are the only key transportation hubs for opening up trade between China and foreign countries and nurturing the local economy. The fact that Northeast China presents such a prosperous and growing scene today cannot be said to be unrelated to these two railways. However, since the sovereignty of the railways is not in our hands, their various policies and measures often do not fully conform to local conditions. Taking the freight rate as an example, its high level is often enough to put industry and commerce at a disadvantage. In the era of stable gold prices, our industrialists and merchants could still endure the pain. However, since the soaring gold prices last year, due to both railways using gold coins as their base currency, the rise in freight rates has further prompted local industry, commerce, and all trades to be on the verge of bankruptcy. All domestic specialties have been cut off from the opportunity to export, while other foreign goods have been cut off from the source of import. Finance has no source to be active, industry and commerce have no source to rely on for turnover, and labor has no source to rely on for livelihood. The so-called 'What can they achieve? They will all drown together' is the pressing phenomenon of today. It is recalled that during the European War, when gold prices plummeted, the two railways urgently maintained their own interests and once increased freight rates. Manchukuo currency increased from 1,498 to 2,202, and the Eastern Railway increased from one to two times. At that time, the market price of gold was only 140 taels of silver per ten taels, and gold tickets and gold rubles required 2.45 yuan to exchange for one Harbin dollar. Compared to today, when every ten taels of gold has been raised to over 780 taels and every gold ticket or gold ruble can be exchanged for around three Harbin dollars, the exchange rate of gold and silver is an inverse proportion. The difference between now and then is more than seven times. And the current freight rate, which is higher than in the past, is also equal to this number. In the past, freight rates were increased due to the drop in gold prices. Now, freight rates should be reduced due to the rise in gold prices. This is a matter of fairness. Therefore, in terms of today's gold prices, the freight rates of the two railways should be restored to the old regulations before the European War. Even if it is said that the current situation is different and it is difficult to reduce this amount of silver suddenly, at the very least, the standard for determining freight rates should also be determined according to the gold price of this time last year. Last year, the market price of gold on this day was 480 taels of silver per ten taels, which is more than 60% lower than the current market price of 780 taels. Large factories in the East and West, following the trend of gold and silver fluctuations, have all lowered the prices of their products compared to the past by 30-40%. For example, round and square iron imported from Europe used to be worth 9 gold pounds, but now it has fallen to 6 pounds. Cloth imported from Japan used to be worth 7 gold tickets per bolt, but now it has fallen to 5.1 yuan. Also, coal from Fushun used to be 13.1 gold tickets per ton, but now it has fallen to 9.3 yuan. They are private businesses purely for profit, and their factories and purchasers are able to make turnovers. If the railway, which is responsible for facilitating transportation and developing the economy, only considers its own interests and does not listen to the pain of the local people, it is not allowed by reason. Moreover, the interests of the local people and the railway are closely related. Since the soaring gold prices, freight rates have remained unchanged, causing the people to suffer economically and have to avoid using the railway. Passengers walk on the roads, and goods are entrusted to horses for transportation, severely restoring the old situation of traffic jams decades ago. If the two railways were to make a statistic, they would clearly understand this situation from their income in recent months. The high freight rate is not only unfavorable to the local people, but also unfavorable to the railway itself. For the sake of the two railways, they should also make changes and reduce freight rates to maintain the local economy, which is to maintain the railway itself. The Chamber of Commerce and other organizations, as the leaders of industry and commerce, see the urgency of the market and have to stand up and appeal. They plan to elect representatives to make vigorous protests to the authorities of the two railways in the coming days, and will only stop after achieving their goals. However, in terms of the current situation in Northeast China, demanding the two railways to lower freight rates is only a temporary solution. To plan for the long-term, there should be a more distant plan. The sovereignty of the two railways is not in our hands, as we have said before. If the matter is simply beneficial to the local people, they will naturally not be willing to provide full assistance where there is a conflict of interest with them. Therefore, if we want Northeast China to have a future of unprecedented development, we should urgently build the Harbin-Taonan Railway to relieve the pain of being bound by the two railways. It is said that the distance from Harbin to Taonan, passing through Jianzhou, Daqing and other places, is only a little over a thousand li (about 500 kilometers), and there are no high mountains in the middle, making it easier to lay the railway. It is estimated that 20 million yuan would be sufficient to cover the cost of building this road. This construction cost may be allocated from the treasuries of the three provinces or by raising railway public bonds, which is not a large amount and should not be difficult. Alternatively, we can imitate the story of the Feng-Hai Railway, with the people of the three provinces buying shares to build it. Once the project is completed, the three provinces will be connected, and we can directly regard the Chinese Eastern and South Manchuria Railways as nothing. The Northeast is vast, rich in resources, and has long been known to the world. Taking only special agricultural products as an example, they are often sufficient to supply the needs of countries around the world. With our unlimited special products, we can exchange them for unlimited money. The three provinces should be prosperous and wealthy, with every family well-fed and every person sufficient. But when we examine the reality, it is not so. This is because we cannot control the sovereignty of transportation, and all the benefits that we should have received are repeatedly seized by others. We can only bow our heads and pick up the scraps. For years, the people of the country have been saddened by the economic aggression of imperialism, and Northeast China is at the forefront of this. Our government and people should rise up together, with one heart and one mind, to complete the thousand-plus li railway between Harbin and Taonan as soon as possible. All the products of the three provinces can be transported directly to Huludao via our own route and then distributed to the East and West Oceans. At this time, whether it is our own route, we will consider everything that can develop the local economy and maintain the people's livelihood. Even if the stipulated freight rate is not much different from the Chinese Eastern and South Manchuria Railways, it is still better to supply the income of the people to the country for the sake of the country, rather than handing over the benefits to foreigners. Moreover, in the northern part of the three provinces, there are still 60-70% of the lands that have not been cultivated. In recent years, various public and private parties in the country have repeatedly organized immigration to open up land, but they have been hindered by the railways' unwillingness to provide assistance, and there has been little success to this day. If the Harbin-Taonan Railway is completed, immigration can be realized as soon as possible, not only can the wilderness be completely reclaimed and the resources of the country developed, but also the borders can be strengthened to prevent the covetousness of foreigners. The consolidation of the country's border defense is based on this road. Recently, the Chamber of Commerce and other organizations have repeatedly gathered to discuss countermeasures to save the market. They all agreed that the former is to save the crisis for a while, and the latter is to seek benefits for a hundred years. It is necessary to do both at the same time to be effective. Therefore, we have prepared a document and respectfully request your office to review and forward it to the relevant departments for implementation." Harbin Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Binjiang County Chamber of Commerce, Binjiang Grain Exchange, Harbin Oil Mill Industry Association, Harbin Flour Fire Association, Binjiang Grain Industry Association, Binjiang Timber Merchants Association, Binjiang Sundries Merchants Association.

Recent News from the Jiangsu Provincial Election Office 58

Since the Jiangsu Provincial Election Office for the National Assembly representatives announced the deadline for counties to submit election registers of various organizations, the work has been very busy. The recent situation of the office is recorded as follows:

Submitting Election Registers: The central government stipulates that the county supervisors shall submit the election registers of various organizations to the general supervisor for review of election qualifications. The deadline is from March 6th to March 15th. As the deadline is approaching, the county supervisors are enthusiastically submitting these registers to the office. The counties that have already registered are Jiangdu, Taicang, Wuxian, Yixing, Changshu, Jiading, Kunshan, Jintan, Jiangpu, Wujiang, Lishui, Fengxian, Gaoyou, Haimen, Fengxian, Shanghai, and others.

Holding Office Meetings: The election office, due to the intensity of the work, convened a meeting of all group leaders and section chiefs at the office the day before yesterday afternoon, which was convoked by the secretary-general. Matters such as the distribution of work and the explanation of legal ambiguities for various counties were discussed in detail.

Reviewing Election Qualifications: The election registers of various organizations and members submitted by the counties have exceeded one-fourth of all the counties in the province. There are many registers, and the qualification review is conducted by the review group of the office in separate groups. Two meetings have been held to discuss the review procedures to ensure they are thorough and accurate.

Working as Usual on Holidays: The office has been working overtime recently due to the heavy workload. In addition to working as usual on holidays, it also works an additional three hours every night. Even on the Memorial Day for the Martyrs of the Northern Expedition the day before yesterday, it did not stop working. Today is the anniversary of the death of the late premier, and the provincial authorities are holding a grand memorial ceremony and, following past practice, a tree-planting ceremony. All agencies are closed for the holiday, but General Supervisor Hu Pu'an issued a hand order stating that all office staff should work as usual because the election is imminent, so the office is not closed today.

Local Dispatches

Songjiang 59

Memorial for the Sixth Anniversary of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Death: Today (the 12th) at 9 a.m., the party, government, military, police, and various organizations in the county held a memorial service for the sixth anniversary of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's death at the public sports field. Thousands of people attended. The ceremony was presided over by a member of the county party department, who read the testament. After the ceremony, a ceremony was held to commemorate the fallen soldiers, presided over by the chairman of the County Consolidation Association. In the afternoon at 1 p.m., a tree-planting ceremony was held. Various organizations planted trees in the Zhongshan Forest at Yuhuang Pavilion. The ceremony was held on the stone altar of Yuhuang Pavilion, and then the participants dispersed at Malu Bridge.

A Local Security Guard Robbed: Yao Xingsheng, a local security guard in Xiangsi Tu, Erqu near Desheng Port, was robbed. His daughter was about to get married, and the trousseau was mostly prepared. Unexpectedly, at about 1 a.m. on the 11th, eight robbers suddenly came, led by someone with a handgun, and broke into the house, taking away all the trousseau and other items, resulting in a loss of several hundred yuan. The victim has reported the incident to the nearby 4th District branch station for investigation. The Public Security Bureau has uncovered a large gambling den in Xinqiao. The County Public Security Bureau recently reported that gambling is rampant in Xinqiao, with various forms such as dice and pai gow. The bureau sent 12 police officers led by officials through a small road to raid the town the night before last. As expected, they found a crowd gambling wildly in a certain tea house, just as they were shouting numbers. Seeing that there were not many police officers, the gamblers closed the gate, intending to resist. Fortunately, the police officers all had box guns to show off, so no major disaster occurred. The owner, Zhou, and more than a dozen gamblers were arrested and sent to the Public Security Bureau for punishment yesterday morning.

Kunshan 60

Commemoration of the Sixth Anniversary of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Death: Yesterday (the 12th) was the sixth anniversary of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's death and the tree-planting campaign. A grand meeting was held at the public sports field in front of Ma'anshan at 9 a.m. On that day, about 30,000 people from various organizations, groups, primary and secondary schools, and so on attended. After the meeting, they went to the front of the Huazang Temple on Ma'anshan to hold a tree-planting ceremony, and County Chief Pang and representatives from various organizations and schools personally planted trees to commemorate and promote the campaign.

Wuxi 61

Rice Boat Robbed in Panxie Feng: The rice boat belonging to Henglin Haoyongtai, which had loaded over 150 piculs of jingdao, was on the way to the Fengtai Yu Rice Shop in Beitang, Wuxi to be sold, when it passed through the Panxie Feng area near Luoshe. Since it was late at night, the boat was anchored for the night. After 12 o'clock, two boats suddenly approached the rice boat. More than a dozen robbers suddenly jumped out, claiming to be searching for contraband as they boarded the boat and implemented a robbery that lasted about an hour before they fled with the loot. After counting, it was found that over a hundred yuan in cash and other items had been robbed, but the rice was not lost. They already drove to the city yesterday to report to the county.

A Filial Son Commits Suicide after Being Released from Prison: Guo Kunquan, a resident of Bashiqiao Xijie, was about thirty years old. His father had passed away early, and his mother, who was still alive, was over sixty years old. However, Kunquan was naturally arrogant and addicted to bad habits. He often demanded money from his mother. If she didn't comply, he would beat her. Because of this abuse, his mother went to the county to file a complaint a few years ago. After the county government investigated the case, the filial son, Kunquan, was sentenced to one year and three months in prison. Recently, he had been released from prison and still smoked opium and did not repent. However, he was unusually short of money. The day before yesterday, he first cut his throat with scissors and then stabbed his stomach with a sharp knife, immediately bleeding profusely and dying.

Inland River Vessels Must Obtain a Certificate of Operation: The County Construction Bureau received instructions from the Construction Department yesterday and issued the Interim Measures and Forms for the Certificate of Operation of Inland River Vessels. It also stipulated that those who had started operations before December 31, 1920, must apply for a supplementary certificate in accordance with the new regulations by the end of March 1921. Vessels which begin operation after the first day of January, 1921, are not permitted to be open without the approved establishment and the Certificate of Operation having been issued in accordance with the new regulations. Director Mao immediately notified all shipping bureaus to comply.

Changzhou 62

The Strange Disappearance of Three Elementary School Students: Wang Ayu, Jiang Liangda, and He Yuchang, three students from Class B of the first grade of the Wuyi Bureau Qianjie Elementary School, were all about seven or eight years old. They went to school on the morning of the 10th, and suddenly disappeared when the roll was called in the second class. The families went to the school to inquire in the afternoon and learned of their disappearance. The families immediately gathered to discuss and search in Suzhou, Wuxi, Shanghai, and various towns, but they did not return until the afternoon of the 11th without any news. They immediately reported to the Public Security First Branch together with the principal, Qian Ziwei, and asked the police to pay attention. In the evening, the family of Jiang Liangda and Wang Ayu suddenly received a letter from the Second District Police Station of Shanghai, stating that their sons Jiang Liangda and Wang Ayu were being held at the station and should be retrieved with a guarantor. The family of He Yuchang was suddenly sent back by railway police at about 8 p.m. When asked about the circumstances of the student's disappearance, the student said that after purchasing snacks at the school's sales point, he was patted on the head and lost consciousness. Then, on the train, he saw an old man accompanying him who looked quite fierce. Therefore, after this incident occurred, the people in the area paid close attention to it and considered it to be strange.

A Brief Account of the Memorial of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Death: All circles of Wuyi held a memorial service for the sixth anniversary of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's death at the public sports field this morning (the 12th). More than 10,000 people attended. At 2 p.m. in the afternoon, an afforestation campaign and tree-planting ceremony was held in Zhongshan Forest in the western suburbs. Various organizations, groups, and schools planted trees separately. After the ceremony, they paraded to the city and dispersed.

Changshu 63

The Business Plan of the Silver and Money Industry This Year: The silver and money industry in our county suffered a loss of 500,000 yuan last year due to the impact of the collapses. This year, in order to resume business abroad, representatives of the industry held a meeting and decided to revise the business rules and submit them to the county government for record and implementation. However, as the market is about to open and the rules have not yet been approved, the outline of the business has been formulated in ten articles and approved by the industry association. The outline is as follows: (1) All transactions with various industries must be settled in silver accounts, and no transactions in foreign currency are allowed. However, accounts that are not for business purposes are not subject to this restriction, or those that are simply deposited without interest, or those that are deposited for delivery, are also not subject to this restriction. (2) The incoming and outgoing of foreign currency is one percentage point, the incoming and outgoing of dollars is one or two taels per thousand, the incoming and outgoing of small dollars is three fen of silver per ten cents, and the incoming and outgoing of copper coins is thirty wen per yuan. (3) One foreign dollar must be received and paid on the same day and cannot be offset. (4) The date of issuance of the bank drafts is limited to fifteen days for the same industry with the character "Fu" and twenty-five days for the same industry with the character "Lu." (5) The date of issuance of Su Shen and other route tickets is twenty-five days. (6) The dollar of various customer accounts must not exceed the term. (7) The Yang Shen costs one yuan per thousand yuan. (8) The cost of silver and foreign exchange in Suzhou exceeds the term of one day. (9) Every month, the industry follows the public resolution of the 25th of each month and the arrears is calculated. (10) Accounts or industry members who have already defaulted are not allowed to trade with each other. In the future, whenever a default occurs, industry members who have suffered losses should report the detailed situation of the account to the association for identification and to avoid future troubles.

A Large Batch of Opium is Requested to be Handled by the Province: A sand boat carrying a large batch of opium in Daji Bridge, Jiujiang District, in our county was robbed by local ruffians Qian Linlin and others a few days ago. The principal offender, Qian Linlin, was arrested by the Public Security and 357 pounds and eight and a half ounces of opium were recovered. The next day, the case was handed over to the county judicial department for review. After the trial by Shen Chengyuan, each of the criminals still answered as before. As a result, Qian Linlin, Shi Pangshi and three other people were taken into custody. The case is serious and must be submitted to the Civil Affairs Office and the High Court for review.

Jiangyin 64

Important suspect in main case caught in Changzhou. Huang Bingying, a resident of this county, previously accused Yang Bingwei, the former head of the detective team, and team members Wu Shanbao and Chen Xiangbao, etc., to the provincial office of embezzling a large amount of land. Since the plaintiff Huang Bingying returned to his hometown, the defendant Wu Shanbao has voluntarily surrendered. The other day, County Magistrate Li learned that Lu Longbao, a key person involved in the case, was hiding at the "Longda Bowl" shop on Beizhijie Gantang Bridge in Changzhou, at the home of his brother Lu Shengleng. County Magistrate Li immediately sent a quick letter to the Wujin Public Security Bureau Chief Li, who dispatched police to the shop and captured Lu Longbao in the attic on the tenth. Chief Li personally escorted him to Cheng, and County Magistrate Li secretly interrogated him that evening. Qian Abao, who was already in custody, was brought in for cross-examination. Lu Longbao's confession was cunning and evasive, but after strict interrogation by County Magistrate Li, he finally confessed to having ninety-two packages of opium, each weighing about seventy taels. Qian Abao still insisted that there were only fifty-two catties, etc. After the interrogation, he was taken into custody.

Relief center receives municipal charity funds and properties. The Relief Center repeatedly had disputes with the First District Office over the receipt of charity funds and properties from Gongshantang, etc. A few days ago, the Relief Center Committee, upon the order of the County Magistrate, together with Public Security Bureau Chief Chen, went to the First District Office to receive the properties. The District Chief first handed over the detailed list of Gongshantang's canal fields and the documents and books of the municipal properties. 696 land deeds under Gongshantang were handed over. A letter was also sent to the Relief Center, stating that in order to protect the municipal properties, these municipal properties should be owned by the urban area forever and should not be confused with county-owned properties with uncertain ownership. It was requested to forward this to the provincial government for record.

The "Daji" merchant ship encountered an accident. The "Daji" merchant ship of the Dada Company's Shanghai-Yangzhou line left Shanghai for Yangzhou the other day (the 10th). It stayed overnight at Laoshu Sandbar. Yesterday (the 11th) at about 4 PM, when it sailed near Xinsheng Port in Rugao, about eighty li away from Jiangyin, it suddenly caught fire. One account says that the steam boiler exploded. The entire ship sank within minutes. At the time, two merchant ships, one upstream and one downstream, happened to pass by and went to the rescue. Jiangyin Duanshan and the Hucao Port areas saw a wisp of white smoke and the sinking ship from a distance. They immediately telephoned the Dada Company in Huangtiangang to report the incident. It was expected that the "Daji" was on schedule for that day, but it had not arrived at the port by 12 PM (it usually arrives by then). The company immediately sent someone with Director Yuan Me of the Yidu Bureau to Xinsheng Port to investigate. It turned out to be the "Daji." However, the exact loss is still to be reported.

Civil Affairs Department approves the transfer of Gao Xiaosheng from Wuxi to Chengxi Township. Gao Xiaosheng, a bandit causing trouble in the Chengxi Township of the Chengwu two counties, was arrested by the Wujin military police and sent to that county for trial. County Magistrate Li, because the Gao bandit committed many crimes in Cheng, telegraphed the Civil Affairs Department on the (1st) to request that the Wujin County be ordered to allow the extradition of the Gao bandit to Cheng County for trial. The other day, County Magistrate Li received instruction No. 4712 from the Civil Affairs Department regarding the Gao bandit case. County Magistrate Zhang of Wujin had reported it, and it was telegraphed back approving that the bandit be extradited from Cheng for interrogation, and the situation be reported. After receiving the order, County Magistrate Li yesterday instructed Wu Bowen, the head of the political police, to take the document to Changzhou to request County Magistrate Zhang to specify a date for the extradition of the Gao bandit to Cheng, and then dispatch a team to Changzhou to bring him back.

Conflict over land seizure occurred in Jingjiang. Between Liuxu Port and Qixu Port in Jingjiang, late at night on the 8th, as the Taikoo Company's Huangpu downstream ship passed by, a certain security group had a conflict with the water police over land seizure. It was reported that there were more than two hundred catties. Merchants and residents of Baxu Port suddenly heard very dense gunfire and were all awakened from their dreams in panic. Later, after learning about the land seizure situation, order gradually returned.

Zhenjiang 65

Bandit leader Ma Ling, a monk, arrested. In the fourth district of the county, there is a bandit named Ma Ling, a monk, who usually has three to four thousand disciples. He commits all kinds of crimes such as robbery, kidnapping, arson, and murder. Moreover, he is highly skilled, and many people dare not compete with him. The other day, he was drinking tea at the Zuifeng Tea House when the Security Team of the Fourth District learned of his whereabouts through informants. The Fourth Branch of the Clearing and Suppression Bureau of that district led more than a dozen members of the security team to surround the teahouse and capture Ma Ling, the monk, on the spot. They dispatched a team to escort him to the county overnight for punishment.

Yangzhou 66

Township Head slanders Branch Director. Hu Pu'an, Director of the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department, because Gao Jichun, the director of the Seventh Branch of the Jiangdu Public Security Bureau, was accused by Zhen Mayor Yu Shanzhi, Township Head Yin Yucheng, and Party member Du Ruibo of various acts of favoritism and corruption, the County Bureau commissioned Zhang Shiqiu to thoroughly investigate and reply that there was no such thing. Yu and others continued to submit reports to the department, stating the previous reasons, and also submitted separate reports to the County Government, Public Security Bureau, and County Party Department to send personnel to thoroughly investigate each section. The department specially ordered the County Bureau to reassign Huang Shijie, the director of the Ninth Branch, to jointly investigate with Inspector Fan of the Public Security Bureau. Now, according to the report, it is still fabricated, and they have obtained documents from Dong Jingqiu, a Party member and resident of the area, Li Shangzhi, a representative of merchants, Xu Maowen, a representative of the people, and more than twenty other people, proving that Gao Jichun has no favoritism or corruption. Education Fee Management Office to be reorganized. The Jiangdu Education Fee Management Office is now being planned for reorganization by the County Bureau. The method is that the County Magistrate will serve as the Chairman, and the heads of the Finance and Education Bureaus will serve as the Vice-Chairmen. The Chamber of Commerce, banks, and the Money Industry Association will each recommend one person to serve as a committee member to jointly organize. It was also decided to make a loan of 60,000 yuan to match salary payments, with the Finance Bureau collecting education fees on behalf as a fund. The miscellaneous donations and land rents under the education fee items will be separately determined to rectify the methods. Yesterday (the 10th), the county formulated the aforementioned plan and submitted it separately to the Finance and Education Departments for review and approval, and will be implemented upon approval.

Huzhou 67

Meningitis spreads in various villages. Since the beginning of spring, an epidemic has spread extremely rapidly in the Sanliqiao area outside the east gate of the city. Many people have died because medical treatment was not timely. Although the county government sent health assistants to the countryside to administer preventive injections, it was of no avail. It has now spread to Songting Village, Xinmin Village, Guanxi Village, Guanbei Village, Changshu Village, etc., outside the east gate. A large number of people have died in succession within a week, especially in Changshu Village. In view of this, the county government of our county held an emergency epidemic prevention meeting yesterday and decided on two measures for the epidemic in Changshu Village: (1) The Public Security Bureau's health assistant, Zhou Yaodao, will consult with the Gospel Hospital to select and send a doctor and a nurse to Changshu Village for medical treatment. (2) A certain amount of funds will be temporarily paid from the advertising donation item, and the county government will report it for record. It was discussed to form a temporary epidemic prevention team for the epidemic in other places, and the county will submit a list to the Civil Affairs Department of this province to request the dispatch of an epidemic prevention team to Huzhou for prevention and control, and also request the allocation of 2,000 yuan of epidemic prevention funds to meet emergency needs and provide relief.

Hefei 68

All county primary schools suspended for reorganization. The Education Department, based on reports from supervisors and various parties, stated that the primary school education in Hefei was repeatedly in turmoil, and the education funds were controlled and exploited by a small number of people, resulting in insufficient distribution. It has approved the requests from all parties and ordered the Hefei Education Bureau to notify all primary schools and social education institutions that they will be uniformly suspended from this semester. It also ordered the Education Bureau Director to consult with the County Magistrate to properly plan and re-establish two complete primary schools and one complete girls' primary school at appropriate locations in the city. Four complete primary schools will be established at appropriate locations in the four townships, and a number of junior primary schools will be established at appropriate locations in the urban and rural areas. The principals and teachers of all primary schools must be strictly appointed, and those who do not meet the qualifications or have had no achievements in previous school operations or have bad records will not be hired. The Education Bureau has now notified all schools and social education institutions: (1) All equipment, books, and other items to be transferred shall be listed in a clear list and submitted to the bureau along with the seals for verification and dispatch of personnel for takeover. (2) Before the arrival of the custodians dispatched by the bureau, the principals of all schools and the responsible persons of social education institutions shall be responsible for safekeeping. (3) The accumulated arrears of all schools and social education institutions over the years shall be submitted to the current Education Funds Clearing Committee for review and resolution in order to avoid compensation.

Mingguang 69

Eastern Anhui bandits attempt large-scale action. The banditry in eastern Anhui is becoming increasingly rampant. Last night (the 10th), Huangjia'an, Jiashanji, Zhangjialao Camp, Shangxiahong, and Wangbao Lixie villages were again captured, and they are approaching the railway. According to the meat tickets who escaped from the bandit dens, the bandits are also organized according to military formations. Recently, female meat tickets have been made to rush-make military uniforms and flags, and there are many ironware, and there is a plan to cut off the road, loot Mingguang, and occupy Xuyi. The Wang Regiment of the Second Cavalry Division stationed in Mingguang felt that its forces were weak and unable to advance, and had telegraphed the aforementioned news to the division headquarters for review and handling. Tonight, the public groups in Sanjie, Guandian, Shizhu, and this area have sent representatives Li Zhu, etc., to Nansuzhou to meet Zhang Lisheng, the division commander, to request the dispatch of troops to suppress them.

Bengbu 70

Bandits rampant between Henan, Anhui, and Jiangsu. Yang Xieyue, a major bandit in eastern Henan, recently led more than 2,000 bandits to occupy the Yongcheng, Guoyang, and Xiaoxian counties at the junction of the three provinces of Henan, Anhui, and Jiangsu. The people there suffer unbearably from their ravages. Recently, they were severely suppressed by the Seventh Division in Xiaoxian territory and are likely to flee back to eastern Henan. It is reported that the bandits are organized like the military and still fly the flag of the Provisional Fourth Division. It was found that the division was originally Qin Jinlin's mixed army, which was surrounded and disarmed by the Henan National Army in the Luyi and Ningling areas last month. Now, the bandits are still using the name of the Fourth Division to loot everywhere. The bandit leader Yang Xieyue calls himself the commander of the First Brigade of the Provisional Fourth Division, and Zhang Keming is the deputy brigade commander. It is estimated that there are more than 2,000 people. Whenever they arrive at a place, the bandit leaders extort grain and fodder from the local area in the name of false positions, and then continue to loot. It is reported that the Jiangsu and Henan National Army are jointly encircling and suppressing them in order to eliminate them.

Xuzhou 71

Abuse of daughter-in-law leads to arrest pending investigation. Zhao, the daughter-in-law of Zhang Yonggui of Zhu Daqiao in the city, died after taking poison due to abuse by her parents-in-law. The county government conducted an autopsy. Yesterday afternoon at 4 PM, adjudicators Huang Jiazhen and Fu Qi opened the court for trial. Adjudicator Huang believed that Zhang Yonggui and others were indeed suspected and ordered that Zhang Yonggui and his wife be taken into custody pending investigation. His son, Hanzhang, was released on bail.

Local News

Yesterday

Commemoration of the Death of the Premier 72

The entire city mourns unanimously. Yesterday, the Propaganda Department of the Shanghai Special City Party Department commemorated the sixth anniversary of the death of Dr. Sun Yat-sen, the Premier of the Chinese Kuomintang. The Propaganda Department specially convened people from all walks of life in the city to hold a commemorative meeting. It was calculated that 600 representatives arrived. The meeting was reported by Yang Qingyuan, Minister of the Municipal Propaganda Department, on the process of the Premier's death and the efforts we should make. Then Zhu Shujian, Wu Zhihao, etc. gave successive speeches, which were tragic and impassioned, moving the listeners. The various situations are recorded below. Meeting order: (1) Play music. (2) All stand in solemn silence. (3) Sing the party song. (4) Pay the highest respects to the party and national flag and the Premier's portrait. (5) The chairman respectfully reads the Premier's will. (6) Silent dedication. (7) Chairman's report. (8) Speech. (9) Shout slogans. (10) Play music. (11) Adjourn.

Meeting staff: (Chairman Group) Yang Qingyuan, Zhang Qun, Xiong Shihui. (Recorder) Zhou Qinmei. (Master of Ceremonies) Zhang Hanyun. (Reception) Chen Ming, Yuan Qingping, Ding Junchuan. (Executive Secretary) Gu Yufei, Li Erbai, Wu Guangming. Report speech: First, Chairman Yang Qingyuan gave a report (the long speech is omitted). Then, Zhu Shujian, Wu Zhihao, Zou Kexin, etc. gave successive speeches, which moved the listeners greatly. The Garrison Department:

Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, the Songhu Garrison Headquarters held the sixth anniversary commemorative meeting of the Premier's death in the auditorium. The meeting was presided over by Chief of Staff Xu Jinyuan, who performed the ceremony. The chairman's report briefly stated the significance of the sixth anniversary, saying that the Premier had great ambitions, extensive reading, steadfast revolution, and the ability to succeed in a great career. He spoke with much pain and encouraged the attendees, etc. After shouting slogans, the ceremony was completed. He then went to Longhua Temple and Xuehua Park to gather officers and soldiers to hold a tree-planting ceremony, which dispersed at about 2 PM. Municipal Government:

Yesterday, the Shanghai Municipal Government held the sixth anniversary commemorative meeting of the Premier's death at 9:00 AM. The Secretary-General, bureau chiefs, staff members, and trainees from the local autonomy training center, totaling more than 400 people, attended the meeting. The Mayor, as the chairman, delivered a speech, which is recorded as follows: Today is the sixth anniversary of the Premier's death. In this sorrowful and solemn day, everyone must have a feeling of grief for the Premier that deepens with each passing day. Brothers also feel the same way. Recalling last year today, when we held the fifth anniversary commemoration here, brothers said that the Premier's great personality and noble achievements, we should admire him, and also said that the Premier's birthday is the beginning of all revolutionary memorial days, and the Premier's death anniversary is an important part of the national revolutionary history, we should deeply commemorate it, and we must clearly understand the Premier's unfinished ambitions, unfulfilled wishes, and the responsibilities entrusted to the people of Jin, and how to strive to realize them. Director Pan's speech on that day put forward the Premier's proposition of peace and struggle to save China to awaken our attention. Now another year has passed, and we think about it with great shame, because since the fifth anniversary was held last year, our revolutionary soldiers have been engaged in the suppression of rebellion, sacrificing countless lives, and the national strength has been achieved. The purpose of national unity is the hope for a solid foundation for the party and the country. The efforts of armed comrades can be said to be worthy of the Premier's mission and can comfort the Premier's spirit in heaven. However, in the political aspect, due to related reasons, we have not been able to strive for construction according to the predetermined procedures. We have to say that this is the most regrettable thing for us. How to make amends and remedy the situation is what we should earnestly recognize and make up our minds to do today in front of the Premier. In terms of our own duties, how to consolidate the foundation of autonomy in this city and how to develop the establishment of Yin in the tutelage period is a matter of course. At the same time, we should also know that the most urgent national issues at present are two: First, the central government convenes the National Congress, and the central government stipulates that the National Congress will be held on May 5. This May 5 is the anniversary of the establishment of the revolutionary government and the inauguration of the Premier as President, and it is of course of great significance. The National Congress is convened based on the Premier's last instructions, as everyone knows. In his will, the Premier entrusted us to promote its realization in the shortest period of time, but the Premier has been dead for six weeks, and now it is only being convened. This is a very painful thing. The National Congress is to ensure peaceful unification and avoid all future wars. In other words, the National Congress is the hope of our Chinese nation's life, so we should pay close attention to it, gather our efforts to promote its realization. Secondly, we should pay attention to the abolition of unequal treaties. Now the reactionary forces are gradually weakened, but the imperialists continue to infringe on our independence and hinder our construction by political and economic means. If the unequal treaties cannot be abolished, then our country still cannot be free, and our nation still cannot develop. Therefore, the two major events in the Premier's will are the convening of the National Congress and the abolition of unequal treaties, which must be promoted for realization in the shortest period of time. Now that the National Congress is in progress, then we can say that one major event has already started, and of course we have to work hard on the remaining one. If we can work hard from today to achieve the goal, then when we come to commemorate the Premier again next year, we can comfort the Premier's spirit in heaven. I hope that my colleagues and comrades and compatriots across the country will work together and strive to do it.

Yesterday

Holding a Tree Planting Ceremony 73

Over 20,000 People Attended

The fourth annual tree planting ceremony was held yesterday at the intersection of Sanmin Road in the city center. The following is a detailed account of the event.

Preparations: The Social Affairs Bureau invited the Secretariat of the Municipal Government and various city departments to organize the preparatory committee for the fourth annual tree planting ceremony. The members included Zhou Rong from the Municipal Government, Wang Liping from the Finance Bureau, Mei Chengtong from the Public Works Bureau, Bao Bode and Qian Zhongnan from the Social Affairs Bureau, Zhou Yongxing from the Public Utilities Bureau, Cao Sunpu from the Education Bureau, Wang Keyong from the Land Bureau, Chen Xuxi from the Health Bureau, and Zhang Shouchun from the Public Security Bureau, totaling eleven members. They held five meetings to decide on matters such as budget allocation, duty assignments, the creation of tree planting slogans, the compilation of introductory materials on tree planting, the distribution of saplings, transportation to the event, the arrangement of the venue, and the invitation of various government agencies, schools, organizations, and important figures. All preparations were completed in advance, and the location of the tree planting ceremony was set at the intersection of Sanmin and Wuquan Roads, where it was officially held yesterday.

Attendance: The fourth annual tree planting ceremony was held at 2:00 PM yesterday. Attendees included Mayor Zhang, bureau chiefs, various schools and organizations, private individuals, and others, totaling over 20,000 people. Sanmin Road, from the venue to the Songhu Road intersection, was packed with people. It was particularly lively with villagers bringing the elderly and children in droves.

Venue Setup: Arches were erected at the Songhu Road intersection and the Sanmin Road intersection. A ceremonial platform was built at the venue, with three thatched sheds on either side as resting places for guests.

Proceedings: The weather was clear yesterday. Various government agencies, organizations, and private individuals arrived at the venue successively from 12:00 PM. Mayor Zhang and bureau chiefs arrived at 1:30 PM, rested briefly, and then began the ceremony at 2:00 PM. In addition to the usual formalities: (1) Tree planting song was sung; (2) Mayor Zhang delivered an opening speech; (3) Bureau Chief Pan Gongzhan, President Hu Shuhua of Tongji University, Wang Yansong representing the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Deputy Director Cai Wuji of the Commodity Inspection Bureau, and President Liu Zhanen of Shanghai University successively gave speeches; (4) Parade and tree planting; (5) Photographing; (6) Adjournment. The speeches are recorded below.

Mayor Zhang's Speech: Everyone, today is the Shanghai Municipal Government's fourth annual tree planting ceremony. The significance of the tree planting movement has been explained in detail in the speeches and reports at each tree planting ceremony. Simply put, promoting afforestation in the city (1) benefits hygiene; (2) enhances aesthetic sense. Dr. Sun Yat-sen once said that aesthetic sense is closely related to national civilization. Other disaster prevention is also closely related to afforestation. There is no need to elaborate further now. We remember that the first tree planting ceremony held by the Municipal Government was at Xiaomu Bridge, the second at Pudong, and the third at Damu Bridge. Each year, the location was different. This year, however, it was chosen here, which is even more important than in previous years because the facts tell us that the population of Shanghai is increasing year by year, and various events are also progressing year by year. The trend of development is moving northward. In consideration of the actual needs, we must follow this trend of development to formulate the plan for Greater Shanghai. Therefore, the Municipal Government has spent a lot of effort and energy to formulate the new Shanghai city center area. It has now been approved by the central government, and several main roads have already begun construction. The Sanmin-Wuquan Road that you are standing on is 60 meters wide and extends directly to the Huangpu River. This is one of the main roads. When the road is completed, construction of the Municipal Government buildings can begin. It is planned to hold the groundbreaking ceremony in July. The Municipal Government is the highest administrative organ in this city. In the future, all construction in the city center area where the new Municipal Government is located will depend on everyone's joint efforts. Therefore, the roadside trees that enhance the beauty of the city must also be created by everyone together. (Omitted below)

Bureau Chief Pan's Speech: Pan Gongzhan, representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, said, "Dr. Sun Yat-sen instructed us that all work during the period of political tutelage should rely on publicity. Both the Party Headquarters and the government should use publicity methods to make the people of the whole country aware of the importance of building a new China. Dr. Sun Yat-sen also instructed us that the method of publicity should be based on facts, not empty and superficial. Now, we are holding a tree planting ceremony here, and this place is also the city center area determined by the Municipal Government. Its significance is very important. The Municipal Government has, after a long period of consideration, decided to make this place the city center area for many reasons, as Mayor Zhang has just said. Now that various constructions have already begun, the Party Headquarters will, of course, based on the facts, assist the government in completing the construction of Greater Shanghai to meet the needs of all Shanghai citizens. The mayor just said that Sanmin-Wuquan Road is connected to the Huangpu River. If we can complete the construction of the Huangpu River bank, such as warehouses and wharves, on the one hand, and complete all the construction in the city center area on the other hand, within two or three years, we can conclude that the currently prosperous concessions will inevitably decline. At that time, we will not need to take back the concessions, and foreigners will naturally be willing to return them to us. We hope that everyone will work together. (Omitted below)"

Wang Yansong's Speech: Wang Yansong, representative of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, said briefly that in the past, we thought the Greater Shanghai plan was an ideal. Now, the city center roads have begun construction, and other projects are also in the planning stage, which shows that ideal is the mother of fact. We all know that the current concessions are full of dirt and filth, such as prostitution, gambling, and other things that all occur in the concessions, while the Chinese areas are not beneficial. It is even more important for us to work hard to build a new Shanghai.

Cai Wuji's Speech: Cai Wuji, Deputy Director of the Commodity Inspection Bureau, said that the expansion of the Northwest drought shows us the importance of afforestation. The government wants to hold a tree planting ceremony during the Qingming Festival. Its significance is not only to ask everyone to plant trees, but to know that planting trees is to cultivate them. It is especially important. President Liu Zhanen of Shanghai University and President Hu Shuhua of Tongji University successively gave speeches (details omitted).

Tree Planting Ceremony on Two Railways: The Special Party Headquarters of the Beijing-Shanghai, Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways jointly held the Sixth Anniversary Commemoration of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Death and Tree Planting Ceremony at Xujiahui Station yesterday (the 12th) with more than 500 people from the Administration Bureau and affiliated district party headquarters, labor unions, and other groups. The original special train departed from the North Station at 10:20 AM. Due to the large number of temporary participants, additional vehicles were added until the train departed at 10:30 AM. The train arrived at the Xujiahui venue in about 20 minutes, where preparations were already complete. The chairman of the meeting was the Party Headquarters Min Luo, the Railway Bureau Liu Weichi, and the Labor Union Li Dasan, with Shi Wenshi as the master of ceremonies, Tan Gengxin, and Bi Zhenghua as recorders. The order was (1) Ringing the bell to start the meeting (2) Playing mourning music (3) Singing the Party song (4) Paying the highest respect to the national flag and Dr. Sun Yat-sen's portrait (5) Silent tribute for three minutes (6) Chairman's report (7) Reading the eulogy (8) Offering wreaths (9) Speech (10) Playing mourning music (11) Shouting slogans (12) Planting trees (13) Photography (14) Refreshments (15) Adjournment.

Tree Planting Situation in Baoshan: Various circles in Baoshan County held a ceremony in the People's Auditorium in the city at 9:00 AM yesterday to commemorate the sixth anniversary of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's death. More than 600 people from various government agencies, schools, and the public participated. Flags were flown at half-mast in all places. The Daji Steamer Caught Fire 74

The Disaster Occurred at Longjusha, with Many Passenger Casualties: Following the accident of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Xinchang Steamer, another accident occurred with the Dada Company's Daji Steamer. At 6:00 PM on the 11th, while traveling to Longjusha, Zhangheng Port, a sudden fire broke out. Many crew members and passengers died. A brief account was in yesterday's Jiangyin urgent telegram. Yesterday, a batch of rescued passengers were brought to Shanghai. The reporter went to the bureau to investigate and the information obtained is recorded as follows:

Departure from Shanghai: The steamer was operating on the Tongyang route. It departed from Shanghai at 12:00 PM on the 10th, going upstream to Tongyang. The ship was loaded with more than 1,000 pieces of white sugar and groceries. There were more than 400 passengers on board. At 5:00 PM on the 11th, the ship passed Yaogang and Rengang and arrived at Tiansheng Port, where it docked to unload cargo. More than 200 Shanghai passengers disembarked, and another 60 newly recruited soldiers from the anti-smuggling camp disembarked to go to Yangzhou. After departing from Tiansheng Port, when the ship was on the Jiangmian of Longjusha, Zhangheng Port, it was about 6:00 PM. At that time, dinner was being served on the ship, and most of the passengers were eating in the main cabin. The ship was still moving when a very loud explosion suddenly occurred in the third-class cabin above the main cabin. The sound of the explosion shook several miles, and disaster struck.

Sulfur Caught Fire: According to the National News Agency, the cause of the accident was said by the personnel of the Customs survey ship "Zhuantiao" who went to the rescue at that time. When the Daji left Shanghai and sailed to Tongzhou, 40 new recruits recruited by a certain military agency disembarked to go to Yangzhou for training. At first, they were squatting in the cargo hold, joking and chatting. Soon, they took out cigarettes and smoked them, squatting on the left side of the stern cabin. The upper part of the cabin was covered with cloth, and the lower part was filled with 80 small boxes of sulfur and saltpeter. When the cigarettes were finished, the cigarette butts were dropped unconsciously. They smelled the sulfur smell and tried their best to save themselves, but it was impossible. Therefore, the fire started from there.

Passengers Jumping into the River: The National News Agency reported that 300-400 passengers on the same boat saw smoke sealing the ship and knew that disaster had occurred. They rushed to get out of the cabin, but the crew, fearing that it would be difficult to save the crowd, immediately drove the passengers to the deck. However, the passengers at the bottom of the cabin could not get out because the door was locked. In a short time, the smoke and flames were unbearable. The crew knew that it was difficult to put out the fire, so they opened the bottom cabin to help the passengers to the deck. However, most of the passengers were carrying their wives and children, and they were all ragged peddlers and farmers with no knowledge at all. Suddenly seeing the fire, they were at a loss and jumped into the river in a hurry. Some of them tried to use baskets to float on the water and avoid drowning, but there were too many people and the waves were too big. Those who jumped early were sunk by those who jumped later, and those who jumped later were dragged down by those who fell into the water earlier, so they all perished together. According to a refugee who was rescued, he did not jump into the water until the fire was close to him. At that time, he felt three or four people wriggling under his feet. I am afraid that none of these people have any hope of survival, it is really miserable.

Shipowner Asks for Help: After the tragedy, the shipowner was afraid

Page 10

that the whole ship would sink, so he hurried to the river bank to carry out rescue work. Shipowner Wu Cailiang quickly launched rockets for help after the disaster occurred.

Rescue Situation: The National News Agency reported that when the Daji was on fire and the passengers gathered on the deck, the cries for help had reached the sky. The fishing boats did not dare to go to the rescue because it was getting dark and they were all collecting nets and arresting thieves, and they heard the cries for help. The special patrol boat dispatched by the Customs happened to be berthed near Xingang (about two Chinese miles from the scene of the accident). It heard the echoes of help and saw the smoke rising into the air. It immediately drummed its wheels and drove forward to the scene of the accident. Since it was difficult for the boat to get close, it changed to releasing four small boards to rescue people separately. As a result, about 200 people were rescued. Because most of the people were soaked in cold water, they were unconscious. They were immediately transferred to the special boat in turn and administered with stove fire and brandy, so that those who slowly recovered could be said to be completely alive. As for the seven people who were rescued but did not wake up, five men and two women, they also came to Shanghai on another boat yesterday, taking the Dahe and Longda boats. More than 70 people who returned to Shanghai were also rescued by special boats and transferred to Shanghai. Therefore, the special boat actually rescued about 200 people. Yesterday morning, the boat loaded with dead people and 123 living people arrived in Shanghai. The dead have been handed over to the rescue bureau for photography and coffin burial, and the living have been handed over to the company for aftermath.

Number of Deaths: The National News Agency reported that the number of passengers and crew members of the Daji who died in the fire and drowned in the water could not be confirmed. The Dada Company said that there were not many deaths, but according to the people who came from the special boat who carried out the rescue, the number of deaths was actually close to 100. Based on the number of people who arrived in Shanghai yesterday, the shipowner Wu A'gen was missing and did not return. Only four of the 14 tea servants on the whole ship arrived in Shanghai yesterday, which shows that there were not a few who suffered this catastrophe. A reporter from the National News Agency saw at the wharf that a Jiangbei passenger named Chen Minghai and his mother, wife, and two sisters, a total of five people, only Chen himself survived yesterday. The others were said to have jumped into the river and lost their whereabouts after being frozen. Later, according to the staff of the Dahe boat, the boat sailed to Zhanghuang Port and transferred the people rescued by the special boat to Shanghai. It was heard that ten corpses were salvaged on the shore.

Despicable Fishermen: The National News Agency reported that when the special boat arrived at the scene of the accident to carry out rescue, the fishing boats near the Daji did not save them when they saw them die, but instead grabbed the boxes and cages thrown into the water by the passengers to use as floating objects. The people on the special boat urged them to rescue them, but they did not move. As a result, they came out to force them and stated that anyone who grabbed property would be shot immediately. As a result, seven or eight fishing boats cooperated with two large fishing boats to rescue people separately, and dozens of people were rescued. It can be seen that the desire for profit makes people lose their minds, and they do not save people in danger. Despicable fishermen!

Company Aftermath: The National News Agency reported that the Dada Company received the alarm on the 11th night and immediately sent the Chuting boat from Shanghai to rush there. By noon yesterday, the families of the passengers who had not returned were almost looking forward to it. Therefore, the company again sent the Chuyuan boat with two towed boats, carrying coffins and cold-proof items to provide assistance and prepare to salvage the corpses. As for those who were rescued and arrived in Shanghai without relatives or relatives, the company prepared meals, accommodation, and tea yesterday and sent them to the company and the Chonghai Association to settle down. It is estimated that the Chuxiang and Chuyuan will return in the future to get a decisive solution. Those passengers who wanted to return to their hometown first were also given tickets by the company to take the boat first. The company's managers and others were discussing how to comfort the victims' families yesterday, and they could not make a decision for a while.

The Ship's Hull Was Not Damaged: The company received a follow-up telegram yesterday saying that the upper part of the Daji had been blown away, but the hull below the main cabin was still intact. Whether there was any loss of cargo in the cabins still needed to be investigated before it could be known. The ship is currently moored on the Jiangmian of Longjusha and Wu is assigned to guard it. Yesterday, the Shanghai Bureau also sent the Daqing boat and Zhang Shusheng to investigate. According to Zhang Junyu, the reporter said that according to the reports of the people who came, the engine in the Daji boat had not been destroyed. If the machinery was not damaged, it could still be towed to Shanghai for repair. How the internal parts were difficult to determine at the moment. It would have to wait until after the boat was inspected.

Shipowner Missing: After the accident, the shipowner Wu Caigen first sent a distress signal, but when the customs patrol ship arrived to rescue him, the crew members firmly asked the shipowner Wu to leave the ship and board the ship, but Wu absolutely refused to leave the ship, saying that it was the duty of the shipowner to be with the ship. At the moment, the shipowner Wu has been reported missing, and even the first and second mates are also missing.

Amount of Loss: The National News Agency reported that the loss of the whole Daji was said by the company yesterday that the cost of the ship was more than 200,000 taels, with a deadweight of more than 800 tons. It has been running on the Shanghai-Yangzhou route for nearly ten years. The sugar, cloth, and seafood carried this time were worth more than 100,000. It is not known whether the cargo and passengers were insured, but the company's Daji boat has not been insured for water and fire. Now the Daji is only left with the hull. Whether it will be repaired in the future will have to wait until people are sent to investigate. The total loss of personnel and property must be 500,000 or 600,000 in the future when everything is done.

History of the Ship: The National News Agency reported that the Daji boat was built by Ruirong Factory in 1925, with a weight of 800 tons and a value of more than 200,000 yuan. The loss of this accident is estimated to be more than 500,000 yuan, and the boat has not been insured. What is left now is only a hull, which is still moored in Longjusha near Zhanghuang Port. The company has sent important staff members Zhang Jun and Wang Jun to the scene of the accident on the Chuyuan towed boat last night to inspect and intends to tow the Daji boat back. As for the shipowner of the Daji boat, Wu Shicai (ie Wu A'gen), the cargo room Meng Dingyuan, and the comprador Xu Jingzhai have all fallen into the water and drowned.

Report to the Military Police: Yesterday, the company reported to the Shanghai Water and Land Public Security Bureau, saying that the company's Daji boat sailed upstream to Longjusha at 6:00 PM yesterday and suddenly had an accident. According to the crew members who escaped from the boat, they were having dinner at the time when they suddenly heard a noisy voice in the third-class cabin. They knew there was a fire and immediately stopped the boat to rescue it. Unfortunately, the fire was blazing in all directions, so the fire brigade tried their best to put out the fire but failed. Fortunately, a customs patrol boat happened to sail to the scene and heard the Daji's call for help and immediately tried to rescue it. It is estimated that 120 passengers and crew members were rescued, and then Dahe and first sailed to the scene and successively rescued 65 people. In addition, there were not a few who were rescued by sand boats and swam out. The number of casualties and the cause of the fire have not been found out. After receiving the letter, the company immediately sent the Chuyuan boat to the scene of the accident to carry out rescue matters. Details will be reported later. (Omitted below)

Manager's Report: Yao Jinjian, the manager of the Yangzhou Dada Company who came to Shanghai on the boat, also jumped into the water when the Daji was completely burned, but was rescued by the lifeboat of the customs patrol boat. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday and made a written report to the Dada Company, saying that Yao Jinjian, 39 years old, from Yangzhou, contracted to handle the Yangzhou Dada Step Bureau's manager situation. Because he came to apply for a passenger, he took the Shanghai Daji boat from Dada Wharf at 2:00 AM on the 11th of this month, with about 200 passengers. At Tiansheng Port at 12:30, more than 100 passengers disembarked and more than 10 passengers embarked. There were 100 newly recruited soldiers. At 2:30, the boat sailed from Tiansheng Port to about ten miles from Xingang. At about 5:00, a fire broke out in the paper cargo under the front cabin. The cause was that the new soldiers who boarded at Tiansheng Port threw cigarette butts indiscriminately into the paper cargo cabin. Immediately, the siren sounded six times and the customs patrol boat rescued 119 people and drowned 7 people, 4 men and 1 woman, 1 boy and girl each. Then the Dahe boat came down to the water to rescue more than 100 people. At that time, they were brought back to Shanghai and completely loaded back to Jiangbei on the company's Daqing boat. It is true.

A Large Batch of Gold Bars Shipped to the United States 75

To Remint Gold Coins: According to the National News Agency, the Central Bank will ship a large batch of gold bars worth US$6.5 million to the San Francisco Mint in the United States to be converted into gold coins to avoid the loss of interest on gold bars stored in the vault. Two Railways

Reasons for the Increase in Train Ticket Prices 76

Effective on the 16th, Purely Affected by the Gold Standard: According to news from the Railway Bureau, one of the important issues discussed at the National Commercial Transportation Conference held by the Ministry of Railways was the freight rate. This issue was carefully studied and discussed by railway experts, commercial groups from various provinces and cities, and representatives from various institutions after collecting various materials. The final decision was that the railway should appropriately increase freight rates. The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou letters will be implemented from the 16th of this month, and other routes will be handled successively. The increase in prices has been transferred by the Ministry of Railways to the Executive Yuan for approval. The content of the price increase is roughly a 20% increase in passenger ticket prices and a maximum 20% increase in freight rates, but there are some with lower percentage increases. The increase in railway prices this time is mainly due to the soaring gold prices and the high cost of materials. Even the freight rates of domestic and foreign shipping companies have recently increased by the same percentage. According to reports, the prices of various materials used by the railway have been increasing daily since last year. Among them, the increase of 30% to 50% is the most common, and the increase of rails and various steel products has even reached more than 60%. Therefore, it is estimated that even after the freight rate is increased by 20%, it will only slightly compensate for a portion of the operating costs. The various improvement expenses for the two routes still need to be planned separately. The freight rates of the two routes are still the lowest among the national routes, so the impact of cost losses is more significant than other routes. According to the basic number of ticket prices per kilometer for third-class passengers on various national routes, the Beijing-Hankou, Beijing-Suiyuan, Tianjin-Pukou, and Longhai routes are all 1.7 cents, Beijing-Ningbo is 1.5 cents, Jiaoji is 1.3 cents, and Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo are 1.2 cents. Compared with the Beijing-Hankou, Beijing-Suiyuan, Tianjin-Pukou, and Longhai routes, Beijing-Shanghai is 70% lower, 50% lower than Beijing-Ningbo, and 30% lower than Jiaoji. In terms of freight, taking the freight rate per ton per 50 kilometers of first-class goods in a whole train as an example, Tianjin-Pukou is 3.89 yuan, Jiaoji is 4.08 yuan, Beijing-Ningbo is 2.88 yuan, Beijing-Suiyuan is 3.9045 yuan, Beijing-Shanghai is 1.74 yuan, and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo is 3.754 yuan. Comparing Beijing-Shanghai with various routes, Tianjin-Pukou is about 80% different, Jiaoji is 130%, Beijing-Ningbo is 60%, and Beijing-Suiyuan is 120%. Therefore, even after the increase of 20% in passenger and freight rates, it is still cheaper than other national routes. If the various routes increase their prices in the future, the difference will be even greater. The railway authorities believe that although the price increase this time is to compensate for a portion of the operating cost losses, the railway is a state-run enterprise and is different from ordinary commercial enterprises that purely aim to make profits. Therefore, for goods with already high daily freight rates or weak affordability, if the increase in freight rates is sufficient to hinder the development of agriculture, industry, and commerce and affect the people's living expenses, the percentage of the freight rate increase should still be appropriately reduced based on the actual situation in order to allow various freight rates to be adjusted fairly. In addition, the original transportation surcharge on the two routes is about 5% of the freight rate, which has recently been cancelled by the Ministry of Railways. Therefore, the price increase is 20% in name, but in reality, it is only about 15% higher than before, and the number of those whose increase is less than 20% is even smaller. The Wusong Municipal Committee petitions

To Rectify the Shanghai-Wusong Train 77

Present it to the Municipal Government to request advice from the Railway Department to order the Railway Bureau to expedite the rectification of the Shanghai-Wusong Railway's steam-powered locomotives. In recent months, the train schedules have been frequently delayed, and passengers have complained. Tang Chengzong and Liu Ziwen, members of the Wusong District Municipal Committee, yesterday presented the facts to the Municipal Government, requesting that the Ministry of Railways be advised to order the Railway Bureau to expedite the rectification to maintain transportation. The petition is recorded as follows:

Presenting to the Ministry of Railways to order the Railway Bureau to expedite the rectification of the Shanghai-Wusong Railway train service that does not follow the prescribed schedule, causing great suffering to the public. I humbly ask for your approval. I, the petitioner, investigated the Shanghai-Wusong Railway after the conversion to steam trains which was initially convenient, but gradually became lax, often failing to depart on time, and this has become increasingly serious recently, with delays of up to two or three hours at a time. The suffering of passengers waiting for the train and the crowding is difficult to describe. In addition, after 4:00 PM every day, when the railway factory is off work, there are often two or three hundred workers competing to get on the train, and passengers are left behind. This is usually tolerable, but for example, in mid-February, during the days of wind and snow, the strong and healthy pushed their way onto the train, while the elderly, weak, women, and children were unable to catch the train and suffered miserably, as the committee members witnessed personally. The railway is an unavoidable means of transportation for the people. If it is not rectified for a long time and the public is left to suffer, it will not only affect the reputation of the Railway Bureau but also greatly affect the development of various businesses of the citizens. Therefore, I am presenting the facts and humbly requesting that the Mayor advise the Ministry of Railways to order the Railway Bureau to expedite the rectification to relieve the unavoidable suffering of the public and to ensure the lasting reputation of the entire Railway Bureau.
