Resolution of the Hengda Yarn Factory Strike 82

Workers at the Hengda Yarn Factory in Yangsi Bridge, Pudong, went on strike in protest of the manager, Hu Shaoliang, beating a female worker. To prevent the strike from escalating, the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs instructed the factory to suspend Hu Shaoliang's work until the strike was resolved. The Bureau convened a mediation meeting at 10 AM the day before yesterday (the 11th), and representatives from both labor and management arrived on time. Presided over by staff member Xu Zhi, after a long discussion, both parties agreed and signed a resolution: Manager Hu Shaoliang will be transferred by the factory to another position. Thus, the factory strike came to an end.

Backlash Against Shanghai Public Security Team Arbitrary Detention for Cloth Clothing 83

Requesting provincial and municipal authorities to investigate. Hengxing Cloth Factory in Yangjing Town, Pudong, recently sold 150 bales of cloth clothing to Yong'an Yarn Factory, which were loaded onto a boat around the 4th of this month at Wusong for delivery. On the afternoon of that day, Lu A'gen's boat, while sailing opposite the Meifu Oil Depot, was intercepted by detectives from the Jiangsu Provincial Water Police Corps, who detained the people at Wusong and refused to release them. Hengxing, concerned about business, suffered considerable losses due to the arbitrary detention. It has reported to the Cotton Industry Association and telegraphed the Jiangsu Provincial Government and Civil Affairs Director Hu Pu'an to release the people and goods, while Yong'an Factory, in urgent need of the goods, has reported to the Yarn Factory Association and telegraphed Mayor Zhang and Director Hu to release them. The text of the telegrams is recorded below: (1) To Director Hu Jun of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Civil Affairs: Presenting a case of detention of commercial goods with unclear circumstances, requesting investigation and resolution to reassure merchants and travelers. The association's motorized cotton ginning department member, Zhang Gusheng, manager of Hengxing Cloth Factory, reports selling 150 bales of machine-ginned cloth clothing to Yong'an Yarn Factory in Wusong. On the 4th of this month, Lu A'gen's boat was loaded for delivery to Yong'an Factory. After the boat departed, its whereabouts were unknown, and a search was conducted with no result. A report was made to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau's Water Patrol Team for investigation, and the association was requested to provide assistance. After investigation by the association, it was learned that Lu A'gen's boat and goods had been seized by the Municipal Public Security Bureau's Water Patrol Team but were actually detained by the Water Police Corps of the Fourth District of Jiangsu. It is unclear why the team arbitrarily detained commercial goods. The goods have been detained for many days, causing considerable losses. The factory has been operating for many years and has always been law-abiding. This forced detention appears to be an intentional attempt to extort money. If a thorough investigation is not conducted, how can the safety of commerce be ensured? In addition to reporting to the provincial government, the matter is urgent and requires clarification of the truth behind the detention. Therefore, we are sending a fast mail telegram requesting that you immediately order the Fourth District of Wusong to release Lu A'gen's boat and goods and investigate the matter thoroughly to reassure merchants and travelers. Respectfully, the Shanghai Chinese Cotton Industry Association. (2) To Shanghai Mayor Zhang and Jiangsu Civil Affairs Director Hu: Yong'an Yarn Factory, a member of the association, reports purchasing 150 bales of machine-ginned cloth clothing from Hengxing Cloth Factory in Yangjing Town, Pudong, which were arbitrarily detained on the 5th of this month by the Fourth District Detachment of the Jiangsu Provincial Water Police Corps at Zao浜. The reason is unknown. These goods are urgently needed, causing significant losses. The Detachment arbitrarily exceeded its authority in detaining commercial goods for a long time without announcing any reason or transferring them to judicial authorities for review. There is clearly something untrue about this. We respectfully request that you order the Detachment to release the detained cotton immediately and severely punish them to protect the people and uphold the law. Respectfully, the Chinese Yarn Factory Association.

Active Progress of the "New Kang" Disaster Relief Association 84

Lawyer Wu Jingxiong generously appointed as representative of the bereaved families association. The case of the Merchants Steam Navigation Company's "New Kang" steamer, which sank on July 21, 1929, in the waters off Chengshanjiao, Shandong, after colliding with the Japanese Nissho Mail Steamship Company's "Ryuno Maru," has been repeatedly appealed by the bereaved families association to the National Government for negotiation. It has been nearly two years, and there is still no real solution. The families are crying out, running around, enduring hardship and suffering beyond description. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has already filed a lawsuit with the Shanghai Special District Local Court. The court has summoned the Japanese shipping company once, but they have not complied. The outcome is still unpredictable. The Bereaved Families Association believes that the case's unresolved status is far from comforting the dead and appeasing the living. In addition to hiring Sheng Zhenwei as legal counsel, it has formally appointed Lawyer Wu Jingxiong as litigation agent yesterday. Lawyer Wu has profound legal knowledge and is respected both domestically and internationally. This case is expected to have new developments in the shortest possible time. The families are unanimously grateful for Lawyer Wu's generous appointment as legal counsel. Although the case is already in legal proceedings, the association believes that for the sake of an early resolution, it is still requesting the National Government to lodge a serious protest with the Japanese government and demand compensation for the loss of life and property. At the same time, it is appealing to all national agricultural, industrial, commercial, and academic groups to unite in resistance and assistance until the goal is achieved. It is said that the association will send representatives to Beijing within days for a third petition to the National Government's Executive Yuan, Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Ministry of Communications, and other agencies.

Local News 2

Major Fire in Pudong 86

More than twenty houses burned to the ground. Ma A'hua suffered burns all over his body but survived. At 12:20 PM yesterday, a fire suddenly broke out at Tongsentai Tobacco and Paper Shop, No. 282, Middle Market, Lanmudu, Pudong. Flames soared into the sky, spreading to more than twenty shops on the left, right, and opposite sides of the street. It was not extinguished until about 3 PM. The following are the detailed findings of the investigation:

The fire started from a frying pan. Tongsentai Tobacco and Paper Shop faces east and has been in business for over thirty years. It is a well-funded, leading shop in Pudong. Last year, it rebuilt its premises and reopened in the new four-bay storefront at the original site on December 20 of the lunar calendar. The northernmost bay of the shop was dedicated to making candles, with several frying pans set up. Yesterday at noon, the shop's old steward and other staff were having lunch. Suddenly, the fire burning under the frying pan flared up because no one was watching it. The oil in the pan caught fire and quickly spread to the nearby oil candles. The shop's old candle-making steward, Ma A'hua, saw the fire in the candle room and immediately went inside, intending to put out the fire. However, it was too late, and he was burned all over his body. He was rescued on the spot and managed to save his life.

Water source cut off due to the filling of the canal. The shop's goods were mainly kerosene, soap, matches, paper, and firecrackers, which fueled the fire, causing it to burn more fiercely. In an instant, the fire burst through the roof. With the strong southwest wind, the fire spread to the northeast. When the Pudong Fire Brigade heard the alarm, they drove to the scene. However, because the nearby small canal had been filled in the previous year, the site was far from the Huangpu River, making it difficult to reach. The fire spread to the neighboring shops on the left and right and then to the opposite side of the street. Thick smoke and flames soared into the sky, making it impossible to control. Later, after learning of the fire, fire brigades from various districts in southern Shanghai also dispatched several fire engines and crossed the river by barge to the scene. They connected long hoses to the Huangpu River to pump water to extinguish the fire. At the same time, fire boats from the Customs and the Public Concession also sailed to the Bund and parked, using long hoses to spray water toward the fire. The fire gradually subsided until 3 PM. The inside of the fire was still smoldering, and it was not extinguished until the evening.

Fire burned left, right, and across the street. In addition to the total destruction of the shop, a total of more than twenty neighboring shops on the left, right, and opposite sides of the street were burned. They are listed below: two buildings of Changqing Sauce Garden, one building of Deyu Guan Dim Sum Shop, one building of Zhenchangxiang Shoe Shop, one building of Bantianlu Tea and Food Shop, two buildings of Yufengtai Foreign Goods Shop, one building of Bingxingyuan Water Heater Shop, one building of Deshunzhai Paper Shop, two buildings of Xin Jing Heping Meat Shop, one building of Gongxing Fried Goods Shop, one building of Xielongtai New Clothing Shop, one building of Shishunxing Tofu Shop, one building of Zhangdingtai Barrel Shop, one building of Hongxing Tea Garden, one building of a certain Bamboo Shop, one building of Beihua Shop, one building of Xushunxing Lead Shop, one building of Shunxing Mutton Shop, one building of Zhangshunxing Barrel Shop. Dafeng Clothing Store had its roof burned off, and all goods were water damaged. A total of more than twenty buildings were destroyed.

District Chief Zhang ordered the shop assistants to be detained. Few of the burned shops had fire insurance. Tongsentai, where the fire started, had insurance of over 6,500 taels, which was a relatively small amount. The total loss of buildings is estimated at over 100,000 yuan, and the loss of goods is also in this amount. Afterwards, the representatives were ordered to interrogate the shop assistants to investigate the cause of the fire. Ma A'hua, the old steward of the shop who was burned in the fire, was discharged from the hospital after treatment. It is said that his injuries were minor and he is not in life-threatening danger. Foreign candidate for the Public Concession Board of Directors.

Four People Express Their Political Views 87

Britons Macnaghten and Hughes, Americans Raven and Carney. All generally advocate buying the Dahua. Yesterday, four foreign candidates for the Public Concession Board of Directors of the Shanghai Public Concession, Britons Macnaghten and Hughes, and Americans Raven and Carney, expressed their views to Western reporters. Their statements are recorded as follows:

Mr. Macnaghten: Major General Macnaghten is the current General. His stated political views are roughly as follows: Since the establishment of the Shanghai Municipal Government, the Public Concession Board has been eager to fully cooperate with it to develop this great commercial port in the East. However, I believe that the best cooperation is to allow the Concession authorities to exercise their functions as freely as possible within the scope of municipal administration. When the new Board takes office, Judge Feetham's investigation report should also be completed. Therefore, the next Board of Directors has a heavy responsibility and will cast the fate of the Concession's future based on its experience and judgment. As for the thorny issue of the extra-settlement roads, the Public Concession Board has done everything possible in the past year to seek its early resolution and maintain the status quo before it is resolved. It is hoped that both parties will dispel misunderstandings and reach a satisfactory solution as soon as possible. Last year, the Public Concession Board paid special attention to the development of the education system and the establishment of hospital committees and parks in densely populated areas. The Chinese government has now formulated a factory law and ordered the Public Concession Board to cooperate with the government to improve labor conditions in a feasible manner. However, this cooperation must be carefully considered to ensure its proper development. Therefore, the question for the next Board of Directors is to seek the progress of municipal administration and the prosperity of the local area in harmony and to maintain the inherent reputation and uphold the necessary municipal powers in the exercise of its functions in accordance with established principles.

Raven and Carney: Raven and Carney, both publicly recommended by the American community as candidates for the Board of Directors, do not support the sale of the Public Concession Board's existing sites. However, regarding the acquisition of the Dahua Hotel property, Raven argues that it is appropriate to seize the opportunity to buy it while the land price is increasing daily. The future use can be discussed at leisure after the acquisition. In addition, the population in the eastern and northern districts is tending to become more dense, and park sites should be acquired as soon as possible. Carney argues that the Dahua Hotel issue should be discussed jointly with the issue of increasing parks within the Concession. Taxpayers should first be asked whether they are willing to spend tens of millions of taels to increase parks. If they express their support, then the location issue should be discussed. Currently, the Chinese residents' side is about to express its views, so when it is submitted to the Western taxpayers' meeting in the future, opinions from all parties can be gathered. In addition, Carney also stated that there is an urgent need to facilitate transportation, expand education, and the old Board of Directors has already paid attention to this. It is expected that progress will be made in these two areas this year.

Hughes' Declaration: Mr. Hughes has drafted a long declaration and submitted it to the North China Daily News for publication. It roughly states that the number of directors limited by the Yangjingbang Regulations is too small, and the time available to each director is limited. They can only serve on one committee and should not hold multiple committee positions. The remedy is to hope that taxpayers will nominate more candidates for the Board of Directors and appoint the unsuccessful candidates, according to the number of votes, as members of various group committees to assist the directors' shortcomings. One is to develop the committee system and promote the principle of decentralized management, so that the Board of Directors only becomes a formal approval mechanism, and a monthly meeting is sufficient. If so, representatives of the press can also be allowed to attend and listen. Regarding the issue of municipal openness, it is advocated that a publication committee be formed by one person from the Board of Directors, one person from the General Office, and one or two press representatives, as proposed by the North China Daily News editorial. Currently, Chinese residents and Japanese residents each have a taxpayer association. Unfortunately, the Western community lacks a body to discuss municipal affairs. Before deciding on very important issues, the Public Concession Board may invite taxpayers and representatives of the Chinese taxpayer association to hold informal meetings to solicit opinions. In addition, he strongly supports the proposal to acquire the Dahua property. Hughes does not support the Public Concession Board's actions regarding the closure of the dog racing track. He says that gambling habits have existed for a long time, and it is especially difficult to ban gambling on various games and sports. If you want to ban it, you must use force, which is to forcibly deprive a large part of the people of their legitimate entertainment. I also know deeply the harm of gambling and am willing to eradicate it. The best way to do this is for the authorities to supervise and set rules to make them comply. It seems better to do so than to ban it completely. Hughes advocates less talk on the issue of road construction outside the settlement. The Chinese authorities have used their ingenuity to take advantage of the weak resistance of foreigners to achieve their goals. Now, it is hoped that both parties will reach an agreement to protect the interests of the Chinese and foreign districts and residents within the area concerned. If the Chinese side can guarantee the same conditions as the Concession in terms of land rental, public convenience, and donation of taxes, then it can also accept its superior governance.

Chung Hwa Road

A Woman Strangled to Death 89

False report of suicide to request exemption from autopsy.

The inside story has not yet been clarified.

The Shanghai Local Court Prosecutor's Office received a report yesterday afternoon from Shao Meisheng, a land agent from the 20th map district, stating that a female resident, Xu Lu, had committed suicide in a flat at No. 841, opposite the Minli School on Zhonghua Road, and requesting an autopsy. Xu Shunlu, the deceased's nephew, also submitted a statement requesting exemption from the autopsy. Prosecutor Wu Shixin briefly questioned him, and finding the situation suspicious, ordered that the request not be granted. He ordered the land agent to wait at the scene of the body, awaiting the autopsy. At 3 PM, Prosecutor Wu, accompanied by examiner Shen Xiqing, went to the scene of the autopsy (the house where the deceased lived was only one room, with the front half as a living room and the back half as a bedroom). When the judge arrived at the scene of the body, which was still lying on the bed in the bedroom, Prosecutor Wu stepped forward to examine it. He saw that the deceased, Xu Lu, was lying supine on the bed covered with a cotton quilt. Examiner Shen lifted the cotton quilt and found that the deceased was wearing a striped velvet jacket and white flannel trousers, with black socks on her feet, and the trouser legs tucked into the socks. The trouser belt was still tightly fastened around her waist, and the buttons on her jacket were also quite neat. However, there was a white cotton rope around her neck. After untying and examining it, it was determined that it was not a suicide but that she had been strangled to death before her death. After personally inspecting the scene, Prosecutor Wu found the circumstances suspicious and examined the bedroom all around. He saw two glass windows behind the side of the bed (each window was three pieces of glass). The glass window on the west side was missing a piece of glass at the bottom, and a pile of broken glass was found outside the window. Upon picking it up, it was found that the broken glass was covered with white paper, but the paste was still unusually damp, and the window lock had also been damaged. The judge concluded that the murderer had entered through the back window. Fearing the sound when breaking the glass, he first pasted extremely thick paste on the window and then broke the glass. The judge then ordered the broken glass to be taken back to the court and questioned the deceased's daughter. The daughter, named A'da, ten years old, testified that "I and my younger brother (A'er, eight years old) went to sleep first last night. This morning, a neighbor woke me up, and my mother was already dead." Prosecutor Wu also found three leather suitcases in the living room (two red and one white) and questioned A'da, who said that the suitcases were all placed in the bedroom and did not know how they were moved outside. They were usually locked. The judge obtained a confession and ordered that they be opened one by one. The suitcases were all filled with old clothes, and the lock on one of the suitcases had been pried open. Prosecutor Wu then questioned the deceased's nephew, Xu Shunlu, and reprimanded him for falsely reporting a suicide case involving a major murder, and ordered the deceased's nephew and the land agent to come to the court tomorrow (today) for instructions. Prosecutor Wu also made a detour to the back to inspect the scene before returning to the court by car. The strangulation cord was taken back to the archives by examiner Shen for storage. It is reported that the deceased's husband, Xu Chunhua, ran Xu Chunji's woodworking business in the past, which was quite successful and had some savings. Xu was originally from Zhangjiang Peng, Pudong. He died of illness on September 16 of last year, leaving behind one wife and one concubine. His wife still lives in Zhangjiang Peng, with two daughters who are said to have married. The concubine, Xu Lu, the deceased, was thirty-five years old this year and had two children, a daughter named A'da, ten years old, and a son named A'er, eight years old. Xu Lu was the daughter of Lu Ruixian (Lu used to be a partner at Qiao Zhishan's land agency in the 16th pier and is now eighty years old). When the judge performed the autopsy yesterday, Lu Ruixian still said that my daughter died of a sudden illness. According to neighbors, this morning, because they saw that the deceased's door was wide open and her suitcases and clothes were scattered all over the floor, they suspected that there was a theft, but they did not expect such a tragedy to occur.

Taxpayer Association's Letter Requesting

Strict Closure of Dog Racing Track 90

Members or Gamblers? The Shanghai Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association sent a letter to the Public Concession Board yesterday, stating: "We, representing more than 95% of the Chinese taxpayers within the Concession, have actively opposed the dog gambling track since it appeared in the Concession. Fortunately, although Your Board has delayed for a long time, it has been able to remedy the situation and decided to close both major dog racing tracks on the 31st of this month to maintain the interests of the residents and to show Your Board's hatred of evil and to fulfill its duties. However, we have recently seen reports that the dog gambling track will continue to run dog races, but gamblers will be limited to members. This move is extremely dangerous, because the purpose of dog racing is only to profit from gambling. Therefore, any gambler who enters the track can simply register for free on the membership roster in the gambling track before or temporarily to act as a member, and the park can still hire touts outside to solicit members, which is actually attracting gamblers. The harm of this is too great to be described. We are sending this letter to request that Your Board pay special attention to strictly enforcing the closure order to cut off the source of the disaster and maintain its prestige and strict fulfillment of its duties. This is addressed to the Public Concession Board."

Tongren Fu Yuan Tang

Settlement of Rental Dispute in Sanli 93

Thanks to the mediation of Mr. Wang Yiting and Mr. Du Yuesheng, the property of the Shanghai Charity Group Tongren Fuyuan Hall, located in Sanli, along the Xixinqiao Street, Dongxi Zilaihuo Street, and Dexing Zhizhong Lixian Streets in the French Concession, was completed last winter. After the tenants moved in, they formed a joint association due to the high rent, and elected representatives to request rent reductions and refunds of charity donations from the landlord. They also submitted requests for relief to the Shanghai Municipal Government and the Social Affairs Bureau. Subsequently, the Social Affairs Bureau sent personnel to mediate, and the landlord convened a board meeting, resolving to uniformly reduce the original rent by 20%, collecting at 80% of the original amount, and notified the tenants. The tenants were still not satisfied, requesting a reduction to 70%. Both sides were in disagreement, and the matter remained unresolved. Mr. Wang Yiting, director of the Charity Group, and Mr. Du Yuesheng, Chinese director of the French Concession, stepped in to mediate, convening both parties to discuss a compromise. A compromise was reached to uniformly collect at 75% of the original amount, and other requests were waived. The tenants expressed satisfaction and agreed to abide by the mediators' intentions, immediately paying the rent. Those without leases also proceeded to enter into them. A rental reduction dispute was resolved with a single word from Mr. Wang and Mr. Du, and both parties expressed gratitude. However, the landlord side took out loans to build the houses, and the rent collected, after repaying the loans, was entirely allocated to charitable purposes, with a fixed budget. Now, with a 25% rent reduction, the estimated income for the year is reduced by approximately 50,000 yuan.

French Municipal Council

Newly Established Detention Center for Civil Offenders 94

In the French Concession, civil offenders in the Mixed Court have traditionally been detained in the detention center of the French General Police Department, and then transported to the court for trial. Recently, the French authorities, considering this procedure to be cumbersome, have established a separate detention center for civil offenders on the lower floor of the Municipal Council. Workers have been hired to renovate it, and once completed, the offenders will be moved to the new facility.

Creditors of Riye Bank File Lawsuit 95

Separate filings in the Special District Court and the French Municipal Council. Shareholders and directors are all defendants. Since the death of Huang Chu Jiu, creditors have been filing claims for repayment, and no solution has been reached for two months. It is now known that the four Shanghai lawyers hired by the Municipal Government, Wu Jingxiong, Chen Tingrui, Qin Liankui, and Jiang Yiping, have transferred the registered creditor rights and the Labour Road creditor group committee to the creditor reorganization, and have formally represented these creditors in filing a lawsuit with the Special District Court, accusing all shareholders and directors of the Gongfa Company and Huang Chu Jiu's sons, Xianzhong and Xinyao, of bearing unlimited liability and clearing the debts in the shortest possible time. The complaint was submitted to the French Municipal Council the day before yesterday (the 11th). Some creditors have already filed lawsuits, so another complaint was filed separately, requesting to receive repayment along with general creditors. The original complaint is recorded as follows: For the matter of requesting a judgment for repayment: We, the complainants, are creditors of the defendants and are seeking to recover funds owed by the defendant's Riye Bank (head office and branches) and the Dashijie Amusement Savings Department, totaling 25,813 taels, 8 mace, 3 candareens, and 9 cash, and 1,103,119 yuan, 1 dime, 4 cents, and 7 li. The defendant's Riye Bank and Dashijie Amusement Savings Department have completely ceased payments. It has been found that Gongfa Company is not a limited liability company and has been managed by shareholder Huang Chu Jiu. Huang Chu Jiu has now died, and his heirs are naturally responsible. The plaintiffs do not know the list of directors and shareholders of the company, but it is heard that all these lists are currently held by the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau. It is requested that your court investigate and clarify the matter with the bureau, and then list each shareholder and director separately as defendants in this case, and then supplement and correct the complaint. We now file a lawsuit according to law, requesting that the defendants be held jointly and severally liable for clearing and repaying the amount pursued by the plaintiffs, totaling 25,813 taels, 8 mace, 3 candareens, and 9 cash, and 1,103,119 yuan, 1 dime, 4 cents, and 7 li, and be made to bear the litigation costs.

Three Suicides 96

Young Girl Swallows Opium: Zhang Huanfang, a 15-year-old girl from Anhui, lived at No. 987, Lane 3, Tongqing Lane, Xiaoshadu Road, West Shanghai. Yesterday at 2:30 PM, her mother gave her two yuan to buy something outside. However, she suddenly lost it on the way. She tearfully returned home and told her mother what had happened. She was slightly reprimanded by her mother. Afterwards, Huanfang was overwhelmed with anger and resentment and secretly swallowed opium, attempting suicide. Her family discovered her and rushed her to Baolong Hospital for treatment, but the medicine was ineffective and she died after some time.

Ball Retriever Stabs Himself: Li Zhengyuan, a 31-year-old man from Tongzhou, rented a room at No. 2, Juchang Lane, Shanhai Road. He worked as a ball retriever at the racetrack. Recently, he had been suffering from illness and financial difficulties, and was very depressed. Yesterday around 3:00 PM, he stabbed himself in the abdomen with a knife at home. His large intestine was flowing with blood. He was rushed to Baolong Hospital for treatment, but due to the severity of his injuries, he died around 4:00 PM.

A Monk Swallows Opium: A Fujian monk, with the Buddhist name Tianya, 43 years old, went to a certain room at the Beizhan Xin Hotel on North Zhejiang Road yesterday morning. It is unknown how he suddenly had suicidal thoughts and swallowed opium. At noon, the tea server entered the room to invite him for lunch and saw that the monk's face was pale and he was unconscious. He immediately reported to the Huishi Police Station, and Officer No. 1538 arrived and took him to Tongren Hospital for treatment. He died around 6:00 PM in the evening. Ear, nose, and throat specialist.

Dr. Deng Lanpu of America, was formerly a professor at the Harvard Medical School in Shanghai and practiced medicine in Shanghai for many years. (Twelve)

traveling was difficult. He anchored at the south end of Rihui Port, north of the Shanghai Cement Factory. Dear Editor, We have read a news article on page 4 of your February 8th edition regarding the loss of valuable fur coats during train travel. Our railway has not recently received any letters from passengers claiming the theft of valuable fur coats. We are writing to request that you verify and correct this information. Sincerely, Tianjin-Pukou Railway Administration Committee, To Shanghai Shenbao Newspaper.

Page 13

Education News

Important News 108

Senior High Normal Department

Adding Scout Training Interest

The Ministry of Education, according to the Zhejiang Education Department's presentation of a letter from the Provincial Training Department, requesting to order all senior high normal departments to add scout training, etc., submitted the case for approval. The Ministry of Education instructed, "We have received the presentation. The organization of scouts is not limited to schools, and its curriculum and work are not school assignments. The age of entry is stipulated as twelve to eighteen years old, which is generally students below junior high school. Therefore, scout training is currently implemented in junior high schools, but no credits are given. It is said that due to the lack of scout training personnel, it is proposed to add scout courses and training methods in senior high normal departments. This is feasible. Senior high normal departments of each school should include scout training as an elective course for students who wish to study it. This elective course is to cultivate scout training personnel. Its nature is a vocational subject for normal school students and is different in purpose from the general training of junior high scouts. No credits should be given in junior high school. Here, it should be the same as general elective subjects and credits should be calculated accordingly. Please note."

Ministry Order Preferentially Treating Qinghai Students 109

The Ministry of Education, according to a presentation from National Tsinghua University, based on a letter from Qinghai Provincial First Normal School, requesting that the school's graduate, Han Zhang, be allowed to enroll without examination to further his studies, as the matter is an unprecedented case, may his request be granted? The Ministry of Education instructed, "The presentation has been received. Qing Province is located in a remote area with backward culture, which is the actual situation. The province's student's request for admission without examination is temporarily approved in accordance with Articles 3 (If schools have vacancies, they should accept these students. Those who meet the qualifications and level can be assigned to the appropriate class, otherwise they will be treated as auditors) and 4 (Mongolian and Tibetan auditors admitted by each school who pass the annual examination should be changed to formal students in the class. Those who fail should still be auditors. A certificate of attendance will be given upon completion of the auditing period) of the Regulations for Treating Mongolian and Tibetan Students announced by the Ministry in July of the eighteenth year."

Local

Various Schools 111

Commemorating the Death of the Premier 112

Jinan University: National Jinan University held a memorial ceremony for the sixth anniversary of the Premier's death at 9:25 AM yesterday in the Zhiyuan Hall of the school. The flag was raised at 9:20 AM (because the Premier died at this moment, the school has always held the memorial ceremony for the Premier's death at 9:25 AM as a rule). The Western band played mourning music and entered the hall to perform the ceremony as required. Representatives of the female student association presented flowers. Principal Zheng chaired the meeting, and Yang Yufen and Li Bangdong recorded the proceedings, with Shen Yu as the master of ceremonies. Hundreds of teachers and students attended. Principal Zheng gave a speech on the significance of the commemoration and elaborated on the Premier's will and the efforts that overseas Chinese children should make in the revolutionary position. After the ceremony, trees were planted in different areas around the school. The school's public school also gathered for a photo.

Shanghai University: Shanghai University held a tree-planting ceremony at 8:00 AM yesterday morning. Then, a general meeting of all teachers and students was convened in the auditorium to commemorate the anniversary of the Premier's death. The ceremony was performed as required, with Zhong Liangfang as the master of ceremonies. Next, Principal Liu explained the Premier's spirit of hard work and service and urged the students to take him as an example. Then, he introduced Mr. Pan Gongzhan, director of the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, who gave a speech, saying that the Premier's various excellent spirits of hard work, service, and dedication should be embraced and not forgotten by everyone. However, everyone must know how to learn the Premier's hard work, service, and dedication, which are entirely built on profound knowledge. With profound knowledge, one can work hard, serve, and dedicate oneself. Otherwise, without preparation, it is just empty words. Revolution means fulfilling one's duties, and its greatest purpose is to focus on construction. China today lacks talent and is not enough to meet the needs of construction. Everyone has this happiness and this opportunity, and the greatest responsibility is to seek profound knowledge to prepare for future service and dedication in society. The social world and knowledge are constantly changing and evolving with the times. Young people must know this during their studies. The Premier never left books at any time in his life. He worked so hard and was so studious. Therefore, we should supplement our knowledge and not forget to read during our work, and we should study hard to gain profound knowledge during our studies. This is everyone's greatest responsibility today, and one's career is based on this. His words were inspiring and thought-provoking. After he finished, the principal stood up to thank him and sang "Beautiful China" and dismissed the meeting.

Wusong Famous Schools: Yesterday was the Premier's sixth anniversary. All military and police agencies and schools and factories in Wusong suspended offices, classes, and work for the day to express their mourning. Banquets and entertainment were also suspended. Tree-planting ceremonies were held in various schools and agencies in the morning to commemorate the event. The entire executive committee of the Eighth District Party Department led the members to Tongji Road. The municipal junior high school was led by the principal and faculty to hold a tree-planting ceremony at the municipal second sports field. Wusong Elementary School held it on the school playground, and the Republic Women's School held it on Beishihe Road. The crowd of onlookers was crowded, and the teachers and students were also very enthusiastic due to the clear weather.

Initiated by Chemical Expert Wu Yun Chu

The Poor Education Fund 113

Personally Donated 10,000 Yuan

Chemical expert Mr. Wu Yun Chu is an enthusiastic person. Currently, in order to encourage poor students to study, he initiated the Poor Education Fund and personally donated 10,000 yuan. Preparations have been completed, and the committee members are Xu Peihuang, Cao Shenxia, Hu Shuhua, and others. The office is located at No. 366, Bailu Road, Shanghai. The Poor Education Fund's regulations are recorded below:

1. This fund is named the Poor Education Fund. 2. This fund was initiated by Mr. Wu Yun Chu of Tianchu MSG Factory. In addition to personally donating 10,000 yuan, he will first raise 50,000 yuan to subsidize young people from poor families who are determined to further their studies. 3. This fund will be managed by a committee organized by the initiator to hire a number of people. The detailed rules for the committee's operation will be determined separately. 4. Those who donate more than 1,000 yuan to this fund will be natural members of the fund's committee. 5. Students subsidized by this fund will be limited to high school graduates who have passed the examination. 6. Students receiving subsidies will be temporarily limited to those studying in domestic universities. 7. The school and the subject of study for subsidized students will be determined by the fund's committee. 8. The amount of the annual subsidy received by subsidized students will be determined by the fund's committee. 9. If a subsidized student drops out of school, the fund's committee may recover the subsidies they have received. 10. If a subsidized student's academic performance is not good, the fund's committee may, based on the report of the school where they are studying, stop their subsidy. 11. After graduation, subsidized students must report their occupation and contact address to the fund's committee. There are no other obligations, but they are free to return the subsidy or donate to this fund. 12. These regulations may be amended by the general meeting of the fund's committee. 13. These regulations will be implemented after being approved by the committee.

Statistics from the Municipal Training Department

Results of the Municipal Elementary School Faculty Party Ideology Test 116

168 schools, 938 people

The average score is still satisfactory.

The Training Department of the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Department, in accordance with the regulations on studying and examining Party principles for faculty and staff of schools at all levels promulgated by the Central Government last winter, conducted a test on Party ideology for faculty and staff of municipal primary and secondary schools throughout the city. The results for the five secondary schools have already been statistically compiled and separately notified to the public. There are many elementary schools throughout the city. The Party Education Section of the Training Department assigned the district party departments to send personnel to conduct nearby tests, which were completed one after another. The test papers were individually verified and reviewed, and the scores were compiled and stored. In total, 168 elementary schools with 938 faculty and staff were tested. The results are still satisfactory (with 30 points as the full score). The Training Department has notified them by letter or urged them to improve. The statistics are recorded as follows:

A Word of Insight 124

— Qiu Shui

▲ In reality, a perfect lover is not necessarily an ideal spouse. However, in novels and in women's minds, the two are often confused.

▲ When in love, women observe the men on the other side through rose-colored glasses. However, after marriage, the rose-colored glasses will naturally be removed, so the enthusiasm of both men and women will inevitably be affected a little.

▲ Marriage is a microscope. From it, we can see the true feelings of the other party.

▲ A pair of comfortable shoes, a comfortable soul, and a comfortable love can keep a woman young and extend her life of enjoyment.

▲ To test the true love of a modern woman is not whether she is willing to pray and repent before God for the man on the other side before marriage, but whether she is willing to share poverty with him after marriage.

▲ Generally, modern women hope that every man is as rich as the oil magnate and as good at spending money as the stars in Hollywood.

▲ In hundreds of years, love will no longer be an uncertain thing, marriage will no longer be a coincidence, and divorce will no longer be an inevitability.

▲ The beauty of men lies in their ability to focus on handling their own affairs, and the weakness of women lies in their inability to let go of other people's affairs.

An Explanation of "The Spirit Never Dies" 125

— Qing Qu

Yesterday was the anniversary of the passing of the Premier, and all of our people commemorated it. The reason for expressing respect and not forgetting is to use the four characters "The Spirit Never Dies" as a slogan. It means that although the Premier's physical body has died, his revolutionary ideology and everything else have not died.

In this world, those who breathe, live, and rest, no matter what kind, their longest lifespan is only a few years. From the external point of view, it is called the physical body, and from the internal point of view, it is called the soul. Which is more important? Scholars value their soul and preserve it. This is what our country's historian Sima Qian called the word "death," which has a definition. One is heavier than Mount Tai, and the other is lighter than a feather. Differentiating it carefully and proving it with modern physicists' theory of the indestructibility of matter, it is said that "those who are born and gather here must gather there again after death, and the components and volume will not be reduced." According to this result, death only occupies a fraction of a second, and the reason for being born is an immortal thing that exists forever in the universe. For example, Confucius, Sakyamuni, and Jesus in the world, there is no one who cannot point out their names and admire their people. Their voices and appearances are as if they are living in the present psychology and leaving a deep image, which is a definite proof of immortality. Then there is Hidetsugu, who reverses Spencer and Darwin's theory and argues that "death is a state of human evolution." His claim is also optimistic about the future and regards the present as a fleeting shadow. From this, death is not sad, and why is life happy? And in life, there is a way to die, and in death, there is a good state of immortality. Alas, this can really break through the outlook on life. If the Japanese scholar Oshio Heihachiro scolds the heroic deeds of heroes and elites and calls them "meetings in a dream," then surpassing our country's Taoism and reaching the Western Buddhism cannot be taken as a model.

It has been six weeks since the Premier's death. His body is no longer visible, but his spirit is now as long as the heavens and the earth and shines as brightly as the sun and the moon. People only know that he used revolution as his career, but they do not know that he can put life and death aside. Therefore, even the day of his death is like the year of his birth. Therefore, I wrote this explanation.

The World's Oldest Man 126

— Ming Zhai

The world's oldest man is Turkey's Luo Hai, who was born in Pittoresk City in 1774 and is now 156 years old. His skin is dark and his hair is bald, but he is as energetic as someone in their forties. He gets up at 5:30 every morning and practices gymnastics with spring machinery. Then he eats oatmeal porridge for breakfast. He himself said that he has not tasted meat for 50 years. For lunch, he only eats bread, milk, beans, and vegetables. When he was young, he served in the military and served as a cavalry officer. He once fought with Napoleon's invading army in 1810. From childhood to the present, he has witnessed his motherland changing its owner twelve times. He has collected the history of the Near East countries for 150 years in his chest. He has remarried eleven times in his life. He even had a son when he was one year old. Luo Hai's parents, children, and grandchildren are all long-lived. His eldest son died at the age of 101. According to research by physiologists, his innate inheritance is beyond the ordinary, and his lifestyle is well-regulated and his food is rich in nutrition. It is also possible for him to enjoy a long life.

International Women's Movement Commemoration 127

— Huang Ji-Ping

On the International Women's Movement Memorial Day, the Shanghai Women's Association held a grand memorial meeting. The Women's Youth Ambition Society held a meeting at Fudan Zibin College and invited celebrities to give speeches. I went to listen to the speech with my classmates from Xiamen University, Cai Chun-Qiu and Mrs. Chen Xue-Yi. Ms. Cai is a talented student from the Yenching Research Institute and has in-depth research on the women's movement. She hopes to get a glimpse of the degree of self-consciousness and awareness of the women's circles in Shanghai, so she has high hopes for this trip. When the car arrived in front of the college, the meeting place was already crowded with men and women, with almost no space. The Jinnan Boy Scouts maintained order, and the Fudan female students were responsible for the reception. Although it was crowded, it was orderly. Nearly a thousand listeners, men also accounted for half of them. The walls of the college were full of beautiful pictures and slogans. The work of the students of the Meizhuan was very pleasing to the eye. After the ceremony was performed, the chairman, Ms. Luo Jun, announced the meaning of the commemoration, and then the speeches began.

There were as many as eight speakers in succession, lasting three hours. More than a thousand people craned their necks and listened, maintaining a quiet attitude from beginning to end, which can be said to be commendable. The speeches contained a lot of stimulating content, so-called "tracing the past and encouraging those who come after." Therefore, I recorded what I remembered to prepare for a case. Ms. Guo Zhen-Yi said that women should be free people with thoughts, ideas, rights, and abilities. If women want to obtain the freedom and equality that human beings should have, they can never get it by relying on empty fantasies, and they cannot achieve it by using emotions. They must use their own will and work together to achieve economic, educational, political, legal, and moral equality. Ms. Liu Wang Li-Ming spoke in extremely fluent Mandarin, with a calm attitude, clear and detailed analysis, and profound meaning. She is worthy of being a pioneer in the women's world. She said that today's commemoration is just a memorial service. She was talking about the disorganization and silence of the women's world in our country. There is no organizational ability and little self-awareness. She said that she was overwhelmed with sorrow. She also said that there are very few women who are self-aware in China. I don't know how many millions of women are living in a dark hell. Generally, women who claim to be liberated are drunk and dreaming of death. They only know how to enjoy themselves and ignore the interests of others. Therefore, the current women's world should have a whole organization to go to the people to work. Mr. Pan Gong-Zhan won the full seat with his solemn and serious tone. Mr. Pan advocated that women should do constructive work. The content of the women's movement is based on Dr. Sun Yat-Sen's The Doctrine of Nation-Building, which is divided into three parts, namely, the psychological construction of the women's movement, the material construction of the women's movement, and the social construction of the women's movement. The most touching thing is that women should first do the movement of people, enjoy the rights of people, and obtain the qualifications of the people, and then do the movement of Chinese female citizens. If modern women do not have a complete personality, how can they educate healthy citizens of the future? Secondly, the women's movement is valuable in its universality. Women who receive higher education are pioneers who know before and know before, and know later. Their responsibilities are even more important. If most women are struggling in the lives of prostitutes, and a few pioneers do not help them, then the women's movement will definitely fail. Thirdly, a husband and wife work together to form a prototype of society. Therefore, forming a good family is the foundation for transforming society, and educating children is the greatest contribution and most significant effect of women to the family, society, and country. When Ms. Chen Zhen-Quan gave her speech, her voice was like a loud bell, passionate and慷慨, and she had the spirit of a great man. She painfully stated that women in the past misunderstood freedom (which led to the sharp increase in today's tragic divorce cases and the habit of women tending to be luxurious, extravagant, and promiscuous. They turned a blind eye to the virtues of diligence and thrift). Women should quickly plan remedial measures for this kind of forgetful psychology. She also exposed the weaknesses and misconceptions of women and the failure of past women's movements, which is admirable. Secondly, Mr. Zhu Ying-Peng Zhang Yi's long speeches were also very moving. The meeting was adjourned at 5 o'clock, and the crowd shouted "tired" incessantly.

Wine Spring Brews Tears and Records Deep Sorrow 128

— Ting Bing Sheng

I met a guest in a wine shop, wearing military uniform, with the style of a knight from Yan and Zhao. I was secretly surprised. After consuming half a catty of Huadiao wine, about six jugs, he suddenly roared, scolded the seat, slammed the table, and scolded the so-called justice of the world. Then, he burst into tears, covered his face, and cried bitterly, sobbing incessantly. My heart was moved. Alas, is it also the way of those who are not met by the times and want to vent the repressed and unjust anger in their hearts with wine? So, I secretly asked the waiter if the guest's name was Jiang, a native of Taiping Township, Sheng County. Every time he gets drunk, he stares, grinds his teeth, roars madly, cries bitterly, and cannot control himself. Then, is he also a sad man? The next night, I met him again and gave him my name card. Although his appearance was haggard, he occasionally showed heroism. However, his words were calm, gentle, and approachable. At first, I did not expect that we would meet by chance and he would immediately allow me to express my deep feelings and heart. Mr. Jiang said, I have a younger cousin named Lin Biao. His family was poor and he could not study. When he grew up, he engaged in farming. His father ordered him to marry the second daughter of Zhou Gui-Ting, the head of Kaiyuan Town. After the wedding, the woman had immoral conduct and had an affair with a man named Qian next door. Qian was a bully in the countryside, and Biao did not dare to resist. He advised his wife to no avail. Qian's gang even tried to use axes to chop Biao. Fortunately, he escaped early and was spared. Biao's father, fearing that disaster would come, quickly sent Biao to flee. The family hugged each other and cried. A dog wagged its tail and bit its clothes, refusing to let go. Biao's wife was moved by her conscience and knelt down to pray to God, deeply repenting and willing to follow Biao. After a long time, they settled in Xidouwan Village, Wu Kang County. They met a fellow villager named Qian Xiang-Lin, who recruited workers on the spot. Biao joined his rule, and his wife worked as a maid. They rented a thatched hut to live in. They lived in peace for several days. Soon, Qian discovered their whereabouts. The secret agents traced their tracks as expected. He used a hundred gold to heavily entice Biao's wife. The woman was greedy and was deceived. She deceived Biao by serving Qian. She did not know the ways of the world. At first, she seemed happy, but in the end, she was sad. She bought poison and waited for Biao to return. She smiled and persuaded him to drink it. Biao did not notice and died. Qian had him buried. Biao's wife then carried the coffin back to Sheng and lived in her mother's house. After a year, she lived with Qian like husband and wife. In the middle of November last year, Qian was heavily in debt due to gambling and could not repay it. The creditors sold Biao's wife privately to the Guo family in Shangbai Village, Wu Kang. This matter was really a family scandal that could not be publicized. However, everyone far and near knew about it. I, a passerby, collected evidence and submitted it to the gentry of the county, asking them to redress the injustice. The gentry of the county took Qian's bribe and ignored it. If I wanted to submit it to the government, I would not have the funds and I would definitely lose the case. Alas, sir, is there any justice in the world? After saying this, hot tears splattered down and dripped into the wine glass. He picked up the glass and said to me, "Life is tears!" Recorded by Ting Bing Sheng on March 3, 1920.

Publishing News: The Dafenghao Three-Day Publication, which is mainly run by the Xu Muyun and Xiao Ting brothers, has been published on the anniversary of the Premier's death. The content includes two photos of the Premier's transfer from the Peking Union Medical College Hospital to the Biyun Temple in Xishan. The important figures of various factions in Ping at that time were all photographed, which is quite valuable. The contributors include Shu Sheyu, Zheng Guoyi, You Ban-Du, and Su Shao-Qing. The content is extremely rich. The second issue includes a photo of Mr. Wu Mingyi, the fiancé of Ms. Zhang Biyue, the female student who shot Huang Chang-Dian in the past and committed suicide in the dormitory of Datong University a month ago. Mr. Wu also wrote a self-report, publishing the causes and consequences of Biyue's suicide, which is of great value.

Warmth in the Heart (381) 129

— Bao Tian-Xiao

Chapter Seventeen: Remaining Youthful With Skilled Makeup and Painted Eyebrows; Prolonging Life Without Method, Golden Market for Excellent Horses

Ye Tong-Hou sat on the edge of her bed. Hua Yuan-Chun poked her face out of the quilt, widened her eyes, and looked at Ye Tong-Hou before shaking her head, saying, "There's a sick person's breath in this room, Third Young Master, please stay away from me." She then closed her eyes again and sighed, saying, "My chest feels stuffy." Ye Tong-Hou leaned closer to look and saw that Lao Liu's face was flushed red, as if she had applied rouge. Even though she was sick, she looked even more charming, and her watery eyes looked even bigger. She pointed her slender finger at her mouth, and A-Jin-Jie said, "Sixth Miss wants to drink boiled water?" She closed her eyes and nodded. When the small teapot was brought to her mouth, she refused to drink, and her pale lips twitched, as if she were saying something. A-Jin-Jie then gave Ye San a look, meaning that she was talking nonsense again. She touched her forehead and said, "The fever is still scalding." A-Jin-Jie's hand touched her head, and she seemed startled, jumping up and staring straight at Ye Tong-Hou, saying, "He...he...who is he?" A-Jin-Jie said, "It's Third Young Master Ye, how can you not recognize him?" Hua Lao-Liu let out a shrill smile, saying, "Third Young Master is here? My loved one is here?" As she spoke, she pursed her lips. A-Jin-Jie brought the small teapot closer, and she took a sip of boiled water, sighing deeply, saying, "My mouth feels uncomfortable." Ye San asked, "Is there anything else that's uncomfortable?" She frowned and said, "My whole body is uncomfortable, and my throat is also choking." Ye Tong-Hou saw that something was wrong, and her illness seemed very serious. He asked A-Jin-Jie, "Have you called a doctor?" A-Jin-Jie said, "I called a doctor who is very familiar with them in the store. He seems to have a Beijing accent. He prescribed a dose of medicine, but she vomited it all out." Ye Tong-Hou was a modern person, so he naturally believed in Western medicine. He said, "That kind of doctor from Beijing won't do. I have an acquaintance who works as a Western doctor here. His surname is Pan. I don't know if he's home at this time. It's best if I go and accompany him here myself." A-Jin-Jie said, "I'm sorry to trouble you, Third Young Master, that would be great." Ye Tong-Hou then went to pull this Dr. Pan over. Fortunately, the road wasn't very far, and he was on Xijiaomin Lane. This Dr. Pan was from the same hometown as Ye Tong-Hou and was very sincere and amiable. When he arrived at Hua Yuan-Chun's bed, he asked about her illness. At this time, Hua Yuan-Chun was still awake and told Dr. Pan that her head was dizzy and her chest felt stuffy. Dr. Pan saw that her face was flushed and said, "Light two more Western candles, please. The electric lights in Beijing are really killing people." After the Western candles were lit, Dr. Pan first shone them on her face, then used his fingers to hold her cheeks and looked at her, asking about her throat and saying that he wanted to see her chest. Hua Yuan-Chun heard this and used her strength to unbutton her chest. When two buttons were undone, a pair of full breasts suddenly jumped out.

Gold Market Rebound Trend 130

The situation is extremely complex. Yesterday, March 12th, the gold market rebounded after its previous sharp decline. However, the situation was abnormally chaotic and bizarre. At times, the price fluctuated by several taels, from two to ten taels. Overall, the market changes reached twenty-one or two taels. Looking back, the final rebound was fourteen or five taels. In terms of trading among firms, Zifeng Yongyuan, Qian Changxiang, and the Dalian gang, among others, had more demand than supply. Hengxing Yuanmao Yongrui Kang and others were sellers. The foreign exchange trend was good, and quotes were long and recurring. Overseas silver markets repeatedly reported gains, but American selling intentions were strong. Thus, sentiment rebounded upwards. It seemed that gold prices would soar by more than ten taels in the future, and exchange rates appeared to be easing. There was a retreat once within 695 taels. Afterwards, buyers became excited, and the situation was good, with a sudden sharp rise of more than ten taels. It is now known that a certain bank has already shipped a large quantity of spot goods to be sent overseas. This, combined with the tightening of the exchange ban, has further strengthened the bullish sentiment, causing prices to pierce through the clouds, reaching over 710 taels. Finally, sellers showed reluctance, and there was a slight pullback. This morning, the forecast for large bars is trending downward.

Opening jump of 11.5 taels. This morning, the April opening price was 705 taels, a jump of 11 taels and 5 mace. Although large bars rose by 16/3, and silver prices increased by 8/3, it was still insufficient, and the US was willing to sell at a depreciated price. Moreover, private telegrams reduced by 125, so sentiment was greatly boosted, and there were still many buyers. Subsequently, the price was raised from 703.5 taels to 709.5 taels. Afterwards, Yuanmao, Yongqian, Changxiang, and goods companies all sold, and the market suddenly softened, with a sharp drop of 13 taels, reaching only 695.8 mace. At that time, Qian Changxiang and others re-entered, so it doubled back to a high of seven or eight taels and was taken by Datong. When the June British gold opened at 13,875 shillings, it was 703.5 taels, and the quote was already 125 US dollars. The 25th gold fell by 1.5 points, only falling by 1.5 taels, to 702 taels. Then it was added to 704 taels. Later, because Mitsui issued British gold at 13,937.5, and the Dalian gang sold, it retreated to 696.5 taels. Hengxing Yuan and others bought in, and in just six or seven minutes, it rose to 701 taels.
